### [242] [LoRe: Adaptive Interaction-Evaluation Routing with Per-Step Interaction Budgets for Iterative Graph Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29005)
*Jintao Li,Yong-Yi Wang,Zheng-An Wang,Heng Fan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LoRe 是一种推理阶段的优化方法，通过动态路由机制减少扩散求解器中冗余的交互评估，在保持解质量的同时，大幅提升了大规模组合优化问题的推理速度并显著降低了内存占用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于扩散的组合优化求解器在处理大规模问题时，由于需要重复评估密集的边/因子交互，导致推理时间长且易受内存限制（显存瓶颈）。现有的静态稀疏化方法难以在保证求解质量的同时兼顾计算效率与可扩展性。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为 LoRe 的无需训练的推理阶段封装器。其核心方法是在扩散模型的每一步迭代中，实施交互评估预算控制：摒弃固定的稀疏化策略（如静态 kNN 图），而是根据交互的冲突程度或不确定性动态路由计算，仅评估固定比例的交互。

Result: 在最大独立集（MIS）问题上，LoRe 将可推理的规模扩展了 3 倍以上，实现了约 8 倍的加速和约 12 倍的峰值内存减少。在旅行商问题（TSP）中，在 n=1000 的规模下，LoRe 实现了约 15 倍的加速和 44 倍的内存减少，同时保持了具有竞争力的解质量，并展现了对拓扑变换的零样本鲁棒性。

Conclusion: LoRe 证明了通过在推理过程中动态路由计算来优化基于扩散的组合优化求解器是可行的。该方法通过在不牺牲解质量的前提下，显著降低内存需求和推理时间，解决了大规模组合优化问题中的计算瓶颈，并表现出良好的跨任务通用性和拓扑稳健性。

Abstract: Diffusion-based neural solvers for combinatorial optimization repeatedly re-evaluate dense edge/factor interactions, making inference expensive in wall-clock time and often memory-bound at scale. Inspired by the computational methodologies of many-body physics, we introduce LoRe, a training-free, inference-time drop-in wrapper that enforces per-step interaction-evaluation budgeting: at each iteration, it evaluates only a fixed fraction of interactions by dynamically routing computation to high-conflict or high-uncertainty interactions, instead of using a fixed sparsification (e.g., static kNN graphs or static masks). Under fully inclusive end-to-end wall-clock accounting, LoRe substantially improves scalability on the Maximum Independent Set (MIS) problem, extending feasible inference more than $3\times$ beyond the baseline's out-of-memory limit, delivering a $\sim 8\times$ speedup and a $\sim 12\times$ peak-memory reduction, with solution quality preserved in this regime. Demonstrating cross-task generality on the large-scale Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP) and zero-shot robustness to topology shifts, LoRe achieves a $\sim 15\times$ speedup at $n=1000$ with a $44\times$ memory reduction and competitive tour quality.

</details>


### [243] [Causal Intelligence for Constraint-Aware Intervention Design to Induce State Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29008)
*Zixuan Song,Uwe Mueller,Dimitris V. Manatakis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: COAST（Causally Optimal Actions for State Transitions）是一种新型因果智能框架，通过结合结构因果模型与多目标优化，实现对系统状态转换的精准干预设计，具有机制透明、模块化和领域无关的特点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预测模型多缺乏机制洞察力，且难以提供科学决策框架。作者旨在解决如何通过有针对性的干预，将复杂系统从一个状态高效、稳定地驱动至另一个预定义状态的科学难题。

Method: COAST框架包含以下核心步骤：1. 从源状态和目标状态数据中学习上下文特定的因果图及结构因果模型（SCM）；2. 利用因果分析归因分布偏移（distributional shifts）至机制层面的驱动因素；3. 提出一种新型约束感知多目标优化算法，用于平衡状态转换的有效性、干预的复杂度以及目标状态的稳定性。整个系统采用模块化设计，具备领域无关性。

Result: 在合成基准测试和真实生物数据集上的实验表明，COAST能够成功识别关键的因果驱动因子，并设计出稳健的单靶点或多靶点干预策略，同时提供透明的机制说明以指导后续的实验验证。

Conclusion: COAST提供了一个强大的因果智能框架，不仅能够发现复杂系统中的因果驱动因素，还能设计出兼顾效果、复杂度和稳定性的最优干预策略，为科学研究中的状态转换问题提供了可解释且具有决策支持能力的工具。

Abstract: Driving a system from one state to another through targeted interventions is a fundamental challenge in science, yet most predictive models offer limited mechanistic insight and no principled framework for decision-making. Here we present COAST (Causally Optimal Actions for State Transitions), a causal-intelligence approach for the in-silico design of constrained interventions that induce user-defined state transitions. Given data characterizing source and target states, COAST learns context-specific causal graphs and structural causal models, attributes observed distributional shifts to mechanism-level causal drivers, and introduces a novel constraint-aware multi-objective optimization formulation that balances transition efficacy, intervention complexity, and target-state stability. The approach is modular and domain-agnostic, integrating feature selection, causal discovery, causal modeling, and intervention identification and evaluation through interchangeable components. Across synthetic benchmarks and real biological datasets, COAST recovers key causal drivers and identifies robust single- and multi-target intervention strategies that achieve desired state transitions, accompanied by transparent mechanistic rationales to guide experimental validation.

### [244] [Label-Free Reinforcement Learning via Cross-Model Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29009)
*Matt Gorbett,Hossein Shirazi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出跨模型熵（CME）作为一种无需标签的强化学习奖励信号，通过利用独立验证模型评估生成质量，有效提升了通用大模型在开放域指令遵循任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型强化学习（RL）严重依赖地面真值（如代码、数学）或昂贵的人工偏好数据，且基于自引用（self-referential）的无标签方法易陷入模型自身错误偏差。研究旨在寻找一种既无需人工干预、又能避免模型自洽性陷阱的通用奖励评估机制。

Method: 提出跨模型熵（Cross-Model Entropy, CME）作为强化学习奖励信号。该方法计算生成器模型输出在独立验证模型下的对数似然均值，利用验证模型对生成内容的可预测性来评估其质量。将其集成到GRPO算法中，实现了无需标签的RL后训练。

Result: 在开放域指令遵循任务（UltraFeedback）上，基于CME的奖励机制在四个模型家族（Qwen, Llama, Gemma, OLMo）及三种训练阶段中均显著优于原始基准模型，在AlpacaEval 2.0评估中取得了52.5%至71.4%的胜率（经平局调整）。

Conclusion: CME提供了一种无需人工标注、无需地面真值验证的通用奖励信号，打破了现有RL训练在开放域任务中的瓶颈。实验证明，该方法在多种模型架构和训练阶段均能有效提升指令遵循能力，为大模型的无监督强化学习提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: Post-training large language models with reinforcement learning is bottlenecked by the reward signal. Existing approaches require either ground-truth verifiable rewards, restricting training to domains with automatic correctness checks (e.g., mathematics, code execution), or human preference labels, which are expensive to collect and prone to reward hacking. Recent label-free methods replace ground-truth verifiers with self-referential signals like majority voting or token entropy over a model's own outputs, but risk reinforcing a model's own errors. In this work we propose Cross-Model Entropy (CME), the mean log-likelihood of a generator's response under a separate verifier model, as a label-free reward signal for RL post-training. CME is continuous, training-free, and grounded in the principle that responses a verifier finds unsurprising are likely correct or high quality. Because the verifier is independent of the generator, the signal cannot be gamed through self-consistency. We integrate CME into GRPO with no other changes to the training loop, extending label-free RL to open-ended instruction following -- a regime where self-referential signals are inapplicable or poorly suited. On open-ended instruction following (UltraFeedback prompts, evaluated on AlpacaEval 2.0), CME rewards beat the untrained base in head-to-head LLM-as-Judge comparisons across four model families (Qwen, Llama, Gemma, OLMo) and three training regimes (pretrained, SFT, and instruction-tuned), with tie-adjusted win rates ranging from 52.5% to 71.4%. Code will be released upon publication.

### [245] [Theoretical Foundations and Effective Algorithms for Policy-Aware Simulator Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29032)
*Christoph Dann,Yishay Mansour,Mehryar Mohri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决模型预测误差导致仿真器被“钻空子”的问题，本文提出了一种基于对抗博弈的训练方法，通过优化模型的战略鲁棒性，成功缩小了仿真与现实之间的性能差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）通常依赖最小化预测损失，但这会导致策略利用模型偏差进行“仿真模拟漏洞利用”（simulator exploitation），从而造成仿真环境与真实环境之间的现实鸿沟（reality gap）。

Method: 提出了一种基于零和极小极大博弈（minimax game）的模型学习框架，将模型与对抗性策略进行博弈训练；引入了“误差-MDP对偶性”（Error-MDP duality），通过将最差情况下的策略搜索转化为标准的奖励为一步预测误差的强化学习问题，实现了主动数据选择。

Result: 在连续控制任务中，该方法将关键区域的预测误差降低了1.5至2.2倍，并使得仅在仿真中训练的策略能够达到接近真实环境最优的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的对抗性训练框架能够有效桥接仿真与现实间的鸿沟，通过优化战略鲁棒性而非单一的预测精度，显著提升了策略在真实环境下的泛化能力和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agents typically learn world models by minimizing predictive loss. However, powerful RL optimizers inevitably exploit minor model inaccuracies, leading to simulator exploitation and a reality gap where policies succeed in simulation but fail in the real world. We propose that the objective for learning simulators should be strategic robustness rather than predictive accuracy, and formulate this as a zero-sum minimax game between a model player and an adversarial policy player. We provide a comprehensive theoretical analysis: (1) an online learning guarantee showing the game is learnable with sublinear regret bounds; (2) a tractable critic-based simplification bounding the global policy-value gap by the local critic's loss; and (3) an Error-MDP duality, proving that finding the worst-case policy is formally dual to a standard RL problem where the reward is the one-step critic error. This duality yields a provably convergent active data selection algorithm. Experiments on continuous control tasks demonstrate that our approach reduces prediction error in strategically important regions by $1.5$-$2.2\times$ and enables policies trained purely in simulation to match near-optimal real-world performance.

### [246] [Moment Matching Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29033)
*Yiyan,Liang,Sifei Liu,Weitong Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于得分和流的生成模型虽然表达能力强，但其推理延迟过高，成为强化学习迭代采样过程中的严重计算瓶颈。为了克服这一限制并提升强化学习算法的推理速度与性能，研究者提出了本方法。

Method: 提出了矩匹配 Q 学习（Moment Matching Q-Learning, MoMa QL）框架，该方法利用统计学中的最大均值差异（MMD）技术，通过对所有阶矩统计量施加强正则化，实现了条件得分函数与目标分布之间的分布级匹配。

Result: 实验表明，MoMa QL 在多种 D4RL 任务中表现出与现有算法相当甚至更优的性能，且计算效率更高。此外，通过加速流式策略的动作采样过程，MoMa QL 在离线到在线（offline-to-online）的强化学习任务中展现出更强的适应能力和在线微调效果。

Conclusion: MoMa QL 框架通过在离线强化学习中利用 MMD 技术，成功解决了基于得分和流的生成模型在推理时的高延迟瓶颈，在保证性能的前提下显著提升了计算效率，尤其在需要快速交互的在线微调场景中表现出色。

Abstract: Score-based and flow-based generative models exhibit remarkable expressive capacity in capturing complex distributions, and have been extensively deployed in tasks ranging from image generation to reinforcement learning. Nevertheless, these models suffer from prolonged inference latency, which imposes a significant computational bottleneck in RL with iterative sampling. To overcome this limitation, we propose a new framework named Moment Matching Q-Learning (MoMa QL), which utilizes a technique from statistical hypothesis testing known as maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) that intend to match all orders of statistics between the original and target distribution. By enforcing strong regularization on all moment statistics, this algorithm guarantees distribution-level convergence for conditional score function and remains stable under various hyperparameters. Empirically, we show that our method MoMa QL is more computationally efficient with a comparable if not competitive performance in various D4RL tasks. Remarkably, by accelerating the action sampling process for flow-based policies, MoMa QL demonstrates superior performance in offline-to-online RL tasks because of faster and stronger adaptability for online interactive finetuning.

### [247] [OISD: On-Policy Internal Self-Distillation of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29089)
*Xinyu Liu,Darryl Cherian Jacob,Yang Zhou,Jindong Wang,Pan He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OISD 框架通过将强化学习模型最终层的推理行为和注意力模式蒸馏到中间层，在无需额外特权信息的情况下，显著增强了模型的逻辑推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习后训练方法主要依赖稀疏的最终输出奖励，忽略了模型中间表示中蕴含的丰富预测信号，导致推理过程的优化不充分。

Method: 提出了“在线策略内部自蒸馏”（OISD）框架，通过两个互补机制将最终层的预测信号传递给中间层：一是logit对齐（传递推理行为），二是注意力对齐（传递注意力模式）。该框架配合GRPO算法，采用带符号的优势加权Jensen-Shannon对齐，在保持策略一致性的同时提取信息丰富的中间表示。

Result: 在四个数学推理任务中，OISD 框架相比于强有力的推理基线模型，展现出了显著且一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: OISD 框架通过利用模型内部预测信号，在不依赖外部特权信息的情况下，有效提升了强化学习后训练的推理能力，证明了中间层表示对复杂推理任务的重要性。

Abstract: Recent reinforcement learning (RL) post-training approaches primarily optimize the final output policy using sparse outcome-level rewards, while largely overlooking predictive signals encoded in intermediate representations. In this paper, we introduce a new paradigm called on-policy internal self-distillation and propose the OISD framework, which improves reasoning by transferring on-policy predictive signals from the final layer to intermediate representations. During rollout and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) optimization, the final layer acts as both the policy and a detached internal teacher for selected intermediate layers, which are guided to align with it through two complementary mechanisms: logit alignment, which transfers high-level reasoning behaviors (how to think), and attention alignment, which enforces consistent attention patterns (where to look) from the final layer to the selected intermediate layer, both without requiring external privileged information. Our OISD, together with GRPO, employs signed advantage-weighted Jensen--Shannon alignment to distill informative intermediate representations while preserving policy consistency under a unified acting policy. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of OISD, with substantial and consistent improvements over strong reasoning RL baselines across four mathematical reasoning tasks. The code will be released at https://github.com/THE-MALT-LAB/OISD

</details>


### [248] [When and How Long? The Readout-Mediator Angle in Temporal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29126)
*Shreyas Fadnavis,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Felix Wyss*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究指出线性探测存在严重的假阳性问题：探针虽然能准确解码模型内部信息，但所捕捉到的方向往往并非模型实际推理所用的因果路径。这挑战了当前基于探测的解释方法及安全监控机制的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示线性探测在模型可解释性中的局限性：即一个能完美解码特定信息（如日期）的线性探针，其所捕捉的特征方向可能与模型内部实际执行推理逻辑的因果路径完全无关。

Method: 研究团队比较了基于线性探测（Probe）提取的方向与基于分布式对齐搜索（DAS）发现的因果中介（Mediator）子空间。通过计算两个子空间之间的角度（Readout-mediator angle）并与随机子空间进行对比，验证了正交性。同时，通过切除（Ablation）实验和稀疏自编码器（SAE）分解，分析了特征的语义内容及其对模型输出的因果影响。

Result: 实验发现，探针识别的日期方向与模型执行任务所依赖的因果子空间在几何上是近乎正交的。切除探针方向对模型性能无影响，而切除DAS识别的因果子空间会导致性能崩溃。这种“探针-中介正交性”在不同规模的模型及多种推理任务中具有普适性。

Conclusion: 线性探测（Linear Probes）可能学习到与模型实际计算逻辑完全正交的特征空间。由于探针识别的特征方向与模型因果路径无关，依赖探针作为运行时安全监控手段存在重大局限性，因为它可能在模型实际忽视的方向上报告高置信度。

Abstract: A linear probe can decode a representation almost perfectly and yet be completely irrelevant to how the model uses it. On calendar-date duration reasoning in language models, a $\sin$/$\cos$ probe recovers day-of-year from a layer's activations, yet ablating its direction has no effect on the model's answers -- while ablating a four-dimensional subspace found by Distributed Alignment Search (DAS) at the same layer collapses performance entirely. We measure the angle between these two subspaces -- the \emph{readout-mediator angle} -- and find it indistinguishable from the angle between two random subspaces (the Haar-uniform null), meaning the probe has learned a direction orthogonal to the model's actual computation. Reverse-engineering the circuit reveals why: attention heads route month-grained context through learned QK offsets at ${\pm}30$ and ${\pm}61$ days, and MLPs then convert \emph{when} (absolute date) into \emph{how long} (duration) -- all downstream of the causal subspace the probe never touches. Sparse-autoencoder decomposition confirms the split: probe-aligned and DAS-aligned features encode semantically disjoint concepts with negligible causal overlap. The dissociation replicates across four scales ($1.5$-$9\,$B) and two model families, with preliminary evidence on two further domains (spatial displacement, symbolic arithmetic), suggesting that readout-mediator orthogonality is a general failure mode of probe-based interpretability. This directly undermines proposals to deploy probes as runtime safety monitors: the probe can report high confidence on a direction the model has silently abandoned.

</details>

Abstract: The wide adoption of LLMs has led to their use in great variety of applications and scenarios, such as chatbot assistants and data annotation, creating the need for the models to satisfy certain budget and hardware constraints. This has led to the trend of LLMs being released in batches consisting of similar models of various sizes for the family of models to adhere to as wide of a range of constraints as possible. In this paper, we validate distillation and quantization as a cost-effective way to expand model families to new sizes and hardware formats. Based on the open-recipe Apertus 8B LLM, we produce Apertus-v1.1 - a distilled family of models with up to 4B parameters trained on 1.7T permissive license tokens. ### [250] [Optimal Gap-Dependent Regret for Private Stochastic Decision-Theoretic Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29148)
*Tommaso Cesari,Roberto Colomboni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文解决了一个COLT公开问题，提出了一种在纯差分隐私约束下，针对随机在线学习的无需时间视界的算法，实现了与间隙相关的最优遗憾界 O(log K / Δ_min + log K / ε)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决COLT领域的一个公开问题（由Hu和Mehta提出），即在纯事件级差分隐私（pure-DP）约束下的随机决策理论在线学习中，确定最优的与间隙（gap）相关的遗憾界（regret rate）。现有研究已知该问题的下界，但缺乏一个能够同时满足此下界且无需预知时间视界（horizon-free）的算法。

Method: 本文提出了一种无需预知时间视界（horizon-free）的算法。该算法将时间划分为呈指数级增长的块，在每个块内仅采取单一动作；通过在每个块的前缀上应用指数机制（exponential mechanism）来选择下一个块的动作；利用随机前缀将块遗憾转化为Softmax选择误差的求和，并使用熵势（entropy-potential）论证来控制隐私导致的动作选择代价。

Result: 对于包含 K 个动作、损失在 [0, 1] 之间且最小间隙为 Δ_min 的问题，本文证明了对于任意时间视界 T，算法的累积遗憾界满足 Reg_T ≤ 1000 * (log K / Δ_min + log K / ε)。该结果与已知的下界在数量级上相匹配。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入一种基于指数机制和时间块划分的无需时间视界（horizon-free）的算法，成功解决了COLT公开问题，证明了在纯差分隐私（pure-DP）约束下，在线学习中与间隙相关的最优遗憾界可以达到 O(log K / Δ_min + log K / ε)。

Abstract: We study stochastic decision-theoretic online learning with full information and event-level pure differential privacy. A COLT open problem of Hu and Mehta asks to determine the optimal gap-dependent regret rate for stochastic decision-theoretic online learning under pure event-level differential privacy. For $K$ actions, losses in $[0,1]$, and a unique best action separated from the second-best action by gap $Δ_{\min}$, the known lower bound is of order $
  \frac{\log K}{\min\{Δ_{\min},\varepsilon\}}, $
or equivalently, up to universal constants, of order \[
  \frac{\log K}{Δ_{\min}}+\frac{\log K}{\varepsilon}. \] We give a horizon-free pure-DP algorithm and prove the explicit regret bound \[
  \operatorname{Reg}_T
  \le
  1000 \cdot \left(\frac{\log K}{Δ_{\min}}+\frac{\log K}{\varepsilon}\right) \] for every horizon $T$. The numerical constant is not optimized. The algorithm partitions time into blocks of exponentially increasing size, plays a single action throughout each block, and chooses the next action by an exponential mechanism applied to a data-independent random prefix of the previous block. The random prefix converts block regret into a sum, over all prefix lengths, of softmax selection errors. A single entropy-potential argument controls all privacy-dominated large-gap actions at cost $\log K/\varepsilon$.

</details>


### [251] [RUBRIC-ARROW: Alternating Pointwise Rubric Reward Modeling for LLM Post-training in Non-verifiable Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29156)
*Haoxiang Jiang,Zihan Dong,Tianci Liu,Wanying Wang,Ran Xu,Tony Yu,Linjun Zhang,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RUBRIC-ARROW 是一种新型的奖励建模框架，通过交替优化准则生成与评分过程，解决了现有评价方法在主观任务中的局限性与平局问题，有效提升了 LLM 后训练的奖励对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的逐点奖励建模（Pointwise Reward Modeling）在处理主观、不可验证的任务时难以给出绝对评分；而现有的基于准则（Rubric-based）的方法过度依赖前沿大模型，且由于布尔聚合常导致评价平局，限制了模型的区分能力。

Method: 提出 RUBRIC-ARROW 框架，包含：1. 联合训练准则生成器与准则条件下的判别器；2. 采用基于概率的评分规则以缓解布尔聚合导致的平局问题；3. 在 RL 阶段仅利用成对偏好数据，并结合交替 GRPO（Group Relative Policy Optimization）方案进行训练。

Result: 实验结果显示，RUBRIC-ARROW 在奖励建模准确性上表现出色，并能为下游的大语言模型（LLM）策略后训练带来显著且一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: RUBRIC-ARROW 提供了一种高效的量化评估框架，通过联合训练评分器和准则生成器，成功解决了传统基于准则的评估方法在非验证性场景下的局限性，证明了其在提升奖励模型精度及下游策略性能方面的有效性。

Abstract: Pointwise reward modeling offers critical signals for LLM post-training, yet struggles with absolute scoring in subjective, non-verifiable settings. Rubric-based methods address this by decomposing evaluation into explicit criteria, but existing approaches typically depend on frontier LLMs and suffer from ties caused by hard Boolean aggregation. We present RUBRIC-ARROW, an alternating framework that jointly trains a rubric generator and a rubric-conditioned judge, with its RL stage using only pairwise preference data. Our method couples a probability-based scoring rule that reduces ties with phase-specific preference-based rewards and an alternating GRPO scheme that together train the pointwise evaluator. Extensive experiments show that RUBRIC-ARROW achieves competitive reward-modeling accuracy and yields consistent gains for downstream policy post-training.

### [252] [Parallax: Parameterized Local Linear Attention for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29157)
*Yifei Zuo,Dhruv Pai,Zhichen Zeng,Alec Dewulf,Shuming Hu,Zhaoran Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Parallax，这是一种可扩展的局部线性注意力机制，通过参数化优化和硬件感知的算法设计，解决了传统注意力机制的局限，在保持计算效率的同时，显著提升了大型语言模型的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大模型已成为主流，但核心的注意力机制长期未变。传统的 Softmax 注意力存在偏差-方差权衡上的局限，而原有的局部线性注意力（LLA）因计算和数值稳定性问题难以扩展到大规模模型预训练中。因此，本文旨在解决 LLA 的扩展性难题，以提升模型的记忆和推理能力。

Method: 提出 Parallax：一种参数化的局部线性注意力机制。它移除了传统 LLA 中的数值求解器，引入了探测 KV 协方差的查询投影矩阵，并设计了硬件感知的算法来提升计算强度，使其能够超越 FlashAttention 的性能。

Result: Parallax 在 0.6B 和 1.7B 规模的模型上实现了持续的困惑度优化，并在下游任务中表现出显著优势。其解码内核在多种批大小和上下文长度下，性能匹配或超越了 FlashAttention 2/3，并验证了与 Muon 优化器协同设计带来的性能增益。

Conclusion: Parallax 证明了局部线性注意力机制在大型语言模型中的可扩展性。通过架构与优化器（特别是 Muon）的协同设计，Parallax 实现了比传统 Softmax 注意力更好的权衡，为构建更高效的注意力模型提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have become the central paradigm in artificial intelligence, yet the core computational primitive of attention has remained structurally unchanged. Local Linear Attention (LLA) is an attention mechanism derived from nonparametric statistics in the test-time regression framework. In contrast to prior research on efficient attention variants, LLA upgrades the local constant estimate in softmax attention to a local linear estimate, yielding provably superior bias-variance tradeoffs for associative memory. However, LLA has not been scaled in LLM pretraining due to computational and numerical stability concerns. We introduce Parallax, a parameterized Local Linear Attention that is scalable for LLMs. Parallax eliminates the numerical solver in LLA and learns an extra query-like projector that probes the KV covariance. We place Parallax within a family of attention mechanisms connected by the bandwidth, the probe construction and the affine structure. We propose a hardware-aware algorithm that increases the arithmetic intensity over FlashAttention, shifting attention into a more compute bound regime. Our prototype decode kernel matches or outperforms FlashAttention 2/3 across diverse batch sizes and context lengths. We pretrain Parallax at 0.6B and 1.7B scales and find consistent perplexity improvements throughout pretraining with gains that transfer to downstream benchmarks. The advantage persists under both parameter-matched and compute-matched controls, demonstrating a Pareto improvement. We perform careful pretraining ablations and identify a novel phenomenon whereby Muon unlocks the capacity of Parallax. To our knowledge, this is the first empirical demonstration of strong architecture-optimizer codesign for attention mechanisms in the architecture research literature.

Abstract: Generating realistic graph-structured data is challenging due to discrete connectivity, varying graph sizes, and class-specific structural patterns. However these models still exhibit noticeable deviations such as in degree and spectral distribution when compared to real graphs, indicating that important structural properties are not fully preserved. This work aims to reduce these deviations by refining the graphs produced by an existing GAN-based graph generator framework with a Genetic Algorithm (GA). In the GAN framework, the generator produces both node features and connectivity patterns, while a GNN-based critic evaluates graph realism and class consistency to ensure global structural and class alignment. Building on this foundation, we apply a GA to refine the edges of generated graphs. The refinement process guides synthetic graphs toward closer agreement with real data, while preserving diversity and novelty. Experimental results show that the GA refinement consistently lowers combined Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) compared to the base model, leading to graphs that more closely match real structural patterns. This demonstrates that evolutionary refinement is an effective and flexible way to correct residual structural deviations in GAN-based graph generators, improving their suitability for realistic graph synthesis and data augmentation.

Method: TIMEGATE是一个专门的策略层，旨在管理持续学习过程中的资源预算（包括时间、标注、训练和评估）。其核心机制是生成一个指标可用性信号（M），根据当前任务需求决定进行部分评估还是全面评估，从而实现动态的自适应管理。

Abstract: As machine learning(ML) systems evolve to continual adaptation, each re-training cycle uses compute, annotation, and energy. We introduce TIMEGATE, a policy layer managing adaptation by budgeting time, labeling, training, and evaluation. TIMEGATE emits a metric-availability signal M for partial vs. full-evaluation decisions. We validate: (i) labeling outperforms training by 2.3x on Adult tabular; (ii) it transfers to LLaMA-3.1-8B + QLoRA on SST-2 (accuracy 0.80 to 0.96; M =1 in 35/36 runs); (iii) M is informative, 28-cell sensitivity shows M drops to 0.81 at tight thresholds; (iv) 100-cycle simulation achieves 66% evaluation-compute savings with no silent mis-promotions; (v) 10%-slice evaluation on LLaMA uses 89% less wall-clock and energy on a single H200 (ratios agree to 0.2%).

### [255] [Influence-Guided Symbolic Regression: Scientific Discovery via LLM-Driven Equation Search with Granular Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29184)
*Evgeny S. Saveliev,Samuel Holt,Nabeel Seedat,David L. Bentley,Jim Weatherall,Mihaela van der Schaar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“影响引导符号回归”（IGSR）框架，通过结合大语言模型与基于边际贡献（影响分数）的细粒度反馈，解决了传统符号回归中搜索效率低下及反馈机制不足的问题，并成功将其应用于真实的生物学科研发现中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在符号回归任务中受到搜索策略低效和反馈信号过于粗糙的限制，现有方法多依赖全局均方误差等标量度量，无法识别方程中具体的性能驱动或误差来源部分。

Method: 提出了一种名为“影响引导符号回归”（IGSR）的方法，将方程发现构建为两步迭代过程：1. 大语言模型生成候选基函数；2. 使用“影响分数”（Influence Scores）量化各基函数对泛化准确率的边际贡献。结合蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS），通过评估各组件的贡献度来实现方程结构的系统性修剪与优化，从而在探索新函数形式与利用高影响组件之间取得平衡。

Result: IGSR 在 LLM-SRBench、药理学 PKPD 模型、流行病学模拟及真实基因组数据等多种基准上表现卓越。特别是在生物学案例研究中，IGSR 成功发现了一项关于 DNA 甲基化与 RNA 聚合酶 II 暂停之间的新关系，该假设后续通过湿实验室实验得到了验证。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的 IGSR 框架证明了通过融合大语言模型的生成能力与基于影响力的细粒度评估，能够有效解决符号回归中的搜索效率与反馈粗糙问题。该方法不仅在基准测试中表现优异，更在生物学发现中展现了其实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising avenue for scientific discovery, yet their application to symbolic regression is often constrained by inefficient search strategies and coarse feedback signals. Current methods typically guide LLMs using scalar metrics (e.g., global Mean Squared Error), which fail to identify which components of a proposed equation are driving performance or causing error. We introduce \textit{Influence-Guided Symbolic Regression} (IGSR), a method that frames equation discovery as an iterative two-step process combining diverse term generation with rigorous selection: an LLM generates candidate basis functions $ψ_j(\mathbf{x})$ for a linear model, which are then evaluated using granular influence scores $Δ_j$. These scores quantify each term's marginal contribution to generalization accuracy, enabling an influence-guided pruning process that systematically refines the model structure. Integrating this mechanism into a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) enables navigating the combinatorial search space while balancing exploration of novel functional forms with exploitation of high-influence components. We demonstrate IGSR's effectiveness on a diverse suite of benchmarks, including LLM-SRBench, pharmacological PKPD models, an epidemiological simulation, and real-world genomic data. Notably, we validate the framework's capacity for genuine discovery in a case study using a high-dimensional biological dataset, in which IGSR identified a novel relationship between DNA methylation and RNA Polymerase II pausing; a hypothesis that was subsequently supported via wet-lab experimentation.

### [256] [When RL Suppresses Its Own Vocabulary: Recovering Reasoning Diversity in Puzzle-to-Math Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29190)
*Mayug Maniparambil,Arjun Karuvally,Terrence Sejnowski,Fergal Reid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究通过引入推理基元分析框架，揭示了模型如何将谜题求解中学习到的逻辑迁移至数学领域；证明了仅通过非数学谜题训练并结合新颖性奖励的RLVR，即可实现强劲的数学推理能力提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能提升大语言模型的推理能力，但该能力在不同领域间迁移的具体条件及其内在机制尚不明确。本研究旨在探究模型如何在完全不接触数学题的情况下，通过谜题训练实现数学推理能力的迁移，并分析推理基元（Reasoning Primitives）在该过程中的角色。

Method: 1. 推理基元框架（Reasoning Primitive-level Framework）：结合9类跨度分类器和基元提取技术，将思维链（CoT）轨迹细分为具体的推理基元，以追踪其在不同训练阶段和领域中的演变。
2. 跨领域训练策略：在SFT和RL阶段仅使用约束满足谜题，不含任何数学数据。
3. 新颖性奖励机制（Novelty Bonus）：基于参考模型的困惑度作为信号，奖励多样化的正确思维链轨迹，旨在恢复被强化学习抑制的“假设”与“回溯”等探索性基元。

Result: 1. 谜题SFT诱导产生了推理基元词汇，在OlymMATH-Hard上实现了+7pp的pass@32提升。
2. 基础GSPO通过组合这些基元形成了更长的推理-验证链，额外提升了+6pp。
3. 引入新颖性奖励后，模型恢复了“假设”和“回溯”等探索性基元，进一步提升了+7pp。
4. 最终模型在数学能力上实现了从16.0%到36.0%的显著跨越，完全无需数学数据的介入。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过强化学习结合可验证奖励（RLVR），模型能够实现跨领域的推理能力迁移，即使在训练阶段完全不接触数学问题，也能显著提升数学解题能力。此外，通过引入新颖性奖励（Novelty Bonus）机制，可以有效缓解强化学习导致的推理策略单一化问题，进一步提升模型的复杂推理上限。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning using verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves LLM reasoning, but the conditions under which it transfers across domains -- and why it does so -- remain under-explored. We study cross-domain transfer in a 7B model whose SFT and RL post-training stages use only constraint-satisfaction puzzles, with no mathematics problems in the post-training data. To analyze how transfer emerges, we introduce a reasoning primitive-level framework that combines a 9-class span classifier with motif extraction, allowing us to segment chain-of-thought traces into primitive motifs and track their evolution across training stages and domains. We find that puzzle SFT induces a reasoning-primitive vocabulary, yielding a $+7$pp \texttt{pass@32} gain on OlymMATH-Hard. Vanilla GSPO then composes these primitives into longer compute-verify chains, adding a further $+6$pp. However, this RL stage also suppresses exploratory primitives such as \textit{hypothesize} and \textit{backtrack}. To address this, we introduce a novelty bonus that rewards diverse correct rollouts, using perplexity under the reference model as a signal. This restores recovery primitives during RL and adds a further $+7$pp \texttt{pass@32} relative to vanilla GSPO. Finally, the end-to-end recipe raises the hard-math capability ceiling from $16.0\%$ at the OLMo3-7B-Instruct-SFT base to $36.0\%$, without adding any mathematics problems during the SFT or RL stages.

### [257] [Auditing Training Data in Generative Music Models via Black-Box Membership Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29202)
*Yi Chen Liu,Jiawei Yu,Kexin Cao,Syed Irfan Ali Meerza,Trishika Movva,Jian Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于黑盒审计的方法：首先，通过影子模型生成音频，构建训练样本（成员）与非训练样本（非成员）的对齐数据对；其次，训练一个“音乐审计器”（Music Auditor），利用学习到的特征空间度量候选音频与模型基于标题生成的输出之间的语义及结构对齐差异，从而实现对候选样本是否参与训练的分类判定。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，在仅有黑盒查询权限的情况下，通过检测生成模型与其训练数据之间的语义及结构对齐特征，可以高精度地审计音乐生成模型的训练数据构成。这一成果为解决生成式AI模型在数据溯源、版权合规及透明度方面的问题提供了强有力的技术工具。

Abstract: Recent advances in text-to-music generation enable high-fidelity synthesis of structured musical audio, raising growing concerns about data provenance, consent, and training transparency. These models are typically trained on large-scale corpora with little disclosure, leaving no practical mechanism to verify whether a particular audio sample was included in training. In this paper, we investigate black-box membership inference for generative music models, aiming to determine whether a candidate music sample was used during training, given only query access to the deployed system. Our key insight is that training membership induces systematically stronger semantic and structural alignment between a candidate sample and the model's generation conditioned on its caption. We query the target model with the associated caption and measure the relationship between the candidate audio and the generated output in a learned feature space. To capture features that separate members from non-members, we construct paired examples consisting of each track and its caption-conditioned generation from shadow models, and train a music auditor to classify membership. The auditor captures alignment patterns characteristic of training membership and generalizes to unseen target models in a fully black-box setting without access to model parameters or training metadata. Across multiple state-of-the-art music generators, our method achieves up to 98.6% accuracy, with false-positive and false-negative rates as low as 1.9% and 1.0%, demonstrating that reliable training-data auditing is feasible in realistic deployment scenarios.

</details>


### [258] [Inferring the Size of Large Language Models From Popular Text Memorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29223)
*Ivica Nikolic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仅需通过模型文本输出即可推断大语言模型参数量下限的黑盒分析方法，利用模型对已知文献的记忆能力及其缩放规律，成功揭示了闭源模型的规模层级与不同厂商的战略差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前主流的大型语言模型（LLM）往往不对外披露参数规模，这使得业界难以准确评估模型的性能潜力、计算成本以及开发者的缩放策略。因此，作者旨在寻找一种仅通过模型输出即可推断模型参数规模的黑盒方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于黑盒测试的推断方法，不需要访问模型的权重或架构信息。该方法首先观察模型对广泛存在的已知文本（如经典文学、宗教文献等）的预测能力，构建一个“准确度概况向量”。随后，通过两种互补的技术进行推断：一是成对统计检验，用于对比两个模型规模的大小；二是利用主成分分析（PCA）构建的缩放律估计器，将记忆信号映射为具体的参数量下限。

Result: 在开源模型上验证表明，该方法能可靠地产生准确的参数下限。在对闭源模型（如主流商业模型）的应用中，该研究成功揭示了不同开发者之间在模型规模上的层级关系，并发现不同厂商在模型演进中存在显著的缩放策略分歧：部分厂商倾向于持续增大参数量，而部分厂商则严格限制模型规模以追求特定效率。

Conclusion: 研究表明，尽管大型语言模型（LLM）的参数量通常是保密的，但通过分析模型在已知文本上的记忆能力（即预测准确度），可以系统地推断出其参数量的保守下限。这一研究揭示了不同厂商在模型缩放策略上的差异，证明了即使在API受限的情况下，黑盒模型的设计参数依然是可以被探测的。

Abstract: The parameter counts of the most widely used large language models (LLMs) are often withheld by their developers, leaving model size -- a primary reference point for interpreting capabilities and costs -- largely undisclosed. We propose a black-box method to infer conservative lower bounds on LLM size from generated text outputs alone, requiring nothing beyond the ability to submit text fragments and observe next-token predictions. Our approach is grounded in a key observation: popular, widely-circulated texts -- such as classical literature, religious texts, and foundational documents -- are present in virtually every large-scale pretraining corpus, and how accurately a model predicts the next word across text fragments of varying length is a reliable signal of how much it has memorized them, which in turn is fundamentally limited by its total parameter count. We aggregate this memorization signal across a diverse corpus of texts and fragment lengths into a single accuracy profile vector per model, and build two complementary inference methods on top of it: a pairwise statistical test that determines which of two models is larger, and a scaling-law estimator that extracts a one-dimensional latent index from these vectors via Principal Component Analysis (PCA) to map the aggregated signal to a parameter count. Validated on a broad set of open-weight models, both methods produce accurate and reliable lower bounds. When applied to popular closed-weight models, our framework recovers internal product hierarchies and reveals a clear divergence in industry scaling strategies: while some developers yield significantly higher bounds indicative of large generational parameter growth, others operate under strict parameter ceilings, demonstrating that hidden design choices can be systematically probed even under strict API limitations.

### [259] [BlockBatch: Multi-Scale Consensus Decoding for Efficient Diffusion Language Model Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29233)
*Xiaoyou Wu,Cheng-Jhih Shih,Binfei Ji,Yong Liu,Yingyan,Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对扩散语言模型推理中的块大小选择难题，本文提出了BlockBatch框架，通过并行处理多种块大小分支并结合置信度门控与同步机制，在保持模型精度的同时，显著提升了推理速度并降低了计算代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散语言模型（dLLM）在块级推理中面临“粒度困境”：小块保持了更好的局部条件，但需要更多去噪步数；大块并行度高，但容易产生错误的早期决策。现有方法通常在推理时固定块大小，未能充分利用不同块大小带来的互补性及多样的KV缓存轨迹。

Method: 提出了“BlockBatch”在线推理框架，核心策略包括：1. 并行执行多种不同块大小的分支；2. 采用基于置信度的令牌合并（confidence-gated token merging）机制；3. 实施基于领导者的同步策略；4. 定期进行全序列刷新（periodic full-sequence refreshes）以确保全局KV状态一致。

Result: 在3个典型的dLLM和4个数据集上进行的实验表明，与Fast-dLLM相比，BlockBatch平均减少了26.6%的去噪函数评估（NFE）次数，实现了1.33倍的端到端推理加速，同时保持了同等的生成准确率。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了“块大小多样性”是提升扩散语言模型（dLLM）推理效率的一个极具价值的新维度。通过利用不同块大小分支间的互补性，BlockBatch 提供了一种无需额外训练的通用框架，在保证生成质量的前提下显著降低了推理成本。

Abstract: Diffusion language models (dLLMs) generate text by iteratively denoising multiple token positions in parallel, offering an attractive alternative to strictly autoregressive decoding. In practice, however, block-wise dLLM inference exposes a difficult granularity trade-off: small blocks preserve local conditioning but require many denoising steps, whereas large blocks expose more parallelism but can make premature commitments and accumulate cache error. Existing acceleration methods typically choose a single block size per request, leaving the complementarity among block sizes unused. We show that block size itself is a useful branching dimension. Different block sizes induce related but non-identical KV-cache trajectories: branches often share an initial prefix, bifurcate at semantically decisive positions, and later agree on syntactically lightweight tokens. Motivated by this structure, we propose BlockBatch, a training-free online inference framework that executes multiple block-size branches for the same request inside a batched forward pass. BlockBatch coordinates these branches through confidence-gated token merging, leader-based synchronization, and periodic full-sequence refreshes that re-anchor local block updates to a globally consistent KV state. Across 3 representative dLLMs and 4 datasets, BlockBatch reduces denoising NFEs by 26.6\% on average and achieves a 1.33$\times$ average end-to-end speedup over Fast-dLLM while preserving accuracy. These results identify block-size diversity as a practical and previously underexplored axis for branch-parallel dLLM inference.

</details>


### [260] [KLAS: Using Similarity to Stitch Neural Networks for Improved Accuracy-Efficiency Tradeoffs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29259)
*Debopam Sanyal,Anantharaman Iyer,Alind Khare,Trisha Jain,Akshay Jajoo,Myungjin Lee,Clayton Kerce,Alexey Tumanov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了优化不同部署场景下的精度-效率权衡，本文提出 KLAS 框架，通过计算预训练模型间中间表征的 KL 散度来自动化选择最优的模型拼接配置，相较于传统启发式方法取得了更好的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型拼接方法多依赖于启发式规则来选择拼接配置，导致得到的精度-效率权衡往往不是最优的，且缺乏泛化能力。作者认为需要一种能够显式捕捉并利用预训练模型间表征相似性的方法来改善这一权衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为 KLAS 的自动拼接选择框架。该方法量化并利用不同预训练模型层间表征的 KL 散度，以衡量模型间的相似性，从而在 $O(k^2n^2)$ 的庞大候选空间中筛选出最优的拼接（Stitch）配置，减少了对启发式规则的依赖。

Result: 实验表明，KLAS 在相同的微调成本下显著优化了拼接模型的精度-效率曲线。相比基准方法，在保持相同计算成本的情况下，ImageNet-1K 的 Top-1 准确率最高提升了 1.21%；或者在保持相同准确率的前提下，FLOPs 减少了 1.33 倍。

Conclusion: KLAS 框架通过利用中间表征的 KL 散度，有效地自动化并优化了模型拼接（Stitching）过程中的配置选择，证明了在模型族内利用表征相似性对于提升精度-效率权衡曲线具有关键作用，为资源受限环境下的模型部署提供了更优的方案。

Abstract: Given the wide range of deployment targets, flexible model selection is essential for optimizing performance within a given compute budget. Recent work demonstrates that stitching pretrained models within a model family enables cost-effective interpolation of the accuracy-efficiency tradeoff space. Stitching transforms intermediate activations from one pretrained model into another, producing a new interpolated stitched network. Such networks provide a pool of deployment options along the accuracy-efficiency spectrum. However, existing stitching approaches often yield suboptimal tradeoffs and lack generalizability, as they primarily rely on heuristics to select stitch configurations. We argue that constructing improved accuracy-efficiency tradeoffs requires explicitly capturing and leveraging the similarity between pretrained models being stitched. To this end, we introduce KLAS, a novel stitch selection framework that automates and generalizes stitch selection across model families by leveraging KL divergence between intermediate representations. KLAS identifies the most promising binary stitches from the $O(k^2n^2)$ possibilities for $k$ pretrained models of depth $n$. Through comprehensive experiments, we demonstrate that KLAS improves the accuracy-efficiency curve of stitched models at the same finetuning cost as baselines. KLAS achieves up to $1.21\%$ higher ImageNet-1K top-1 accuracy at the same computational cost, or maintains accuracy with a $1.33\times$ reduction in FLOPs.

In this paper, popular adaptive optimization methods like Adam and AMSGrad are critically reviewed with an emphasis on their fundamental design concepts. ### [262] [Do Physics Foundation Models Learn Generalizable Physics? A Bias-Aware Benchmark Across Physical Regimes and Distribution Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29283)
*Mengdi Chu,Yang Liu,Ayan Biswas,Han-Wei Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了当前物理基础模型在不同物理场景下的泛化能力局限性，指出单纯的规模扩张和数据增加并非通向通用物理智能的唯一途径，必须深入研究更具可迁移性的物理学习机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的物理基础模型评价方式过于单一，常将复杂表现压缩为单一平均分，导致无法区分模型是真正习得了通用物理规律，还是仅在特定数据集上表现良好。研究旨在揭示模型在不同物理体制和复杂性下的真实泛化能力。

Method: 构建了一个包含8种物理动力学、3种训练数据组合及25种测试方案的综合基准（Benchmark）。通过对5种物理基础模型架构（每种包含从头训练和3种不同规模预训练版本）进行总计60,000次测量，系统评估了模型在分布内（ID）、分布偏移（DS）和分布外（OOD）设置下的表现。

Result: 研究发现当前物理基础模型主要表现为“条件通才”而非“通用通才”。模型性能受限于物理体制、时间尺度、初始条件设置、预训练过程及架构差异。增加训练数据的多样性、扩大模型规模或进行预训练，只能部分改善模型性能，无法从根本上消除其对特定领域的偏见。

Conclusion: 现有的物理基础模型并非真正的“通用通才”，其泛化能力高度依赖于物理机制、时间尺度及初始条件等因素。单纯通过增大模型规模或扩展数据难以根本解决这些偏见，未来的研究应转向捕捉跨体制、跨尺度且可迁移的物理知识机制。

Abstract: Recent physics foundation models claim general spatiotemporal forecasting ability, yet their evaluations often collapse performance into a single average score under a fixed training distribution. This makes it difficult to determine whether a model has learned generalizable physical dynamics or only performs well under particular settings. We construct a benchmark with 8 physical dynamics, 3 training-data mixtures, and 25 test regimes induced by dynamic-scale and initial-condition complexity shifts, covering in-distribution, distribution-shift, and out-of-distribution settings. We evaluate five physics foundation model architectures and four model variants per architecture (scratch and three pretrained sizes), resulting in 60,000 measurements. Our results show that current physics foundation models behave as conditional rather than universal generalists: their generality depends on the physical regime, temporal scale, initial-condition setting, pretraining, model size, and architecture. Improving the training data distribution only partially mitigates this limitation. Pretraining and scaling are also unable to reliably remove their ability biases. We argue that improving physics foundation models requires moving beyond scaling models or expanding data, toward learning mechanisms that better capture transferable physical knowledge across regimes, temporal scales, and distribution shifts.

### [263] [Attention as In-Context Empirical Bayes: A Two-Stage View via Particle Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29351)
*Matthew Smart,Soumya Ganguly,Nilava Metya,Alexandre V. Morozov,Anirvan M. Sengupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Transformer的注意力机制本质上是一种基于样本的经验贝叶斯后验推断，并证明了其深度和跳跃连接分别对应于经验分布的优化与后验推断，从而在理论上将Transformer与反向扩散过程联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型在处理各种任务时表现出强大的上下文学习能力，但其内在的统计机制尚不明确。研究者旨在通过分析最小化注意机制下的Transformer模型，揭示深度和注意力残差在上下文推理中扮演的统计角色，并探究它们是否能实现无需显式噪声调度的有效去噪。

Method: 本文采用经验贝叶斯（Empirical Bayes）解释框架，将最小注意力Transformer建模为两阶段处理过程：第一阶段利用粒子动力学（Particle Dynamics）通过深度层优化经验分布；第二阶段通过长程跳跃连接（Skip-connection）将原始噪声输入作为查询项进行后验推断。同时，通过分析核密度估计和能量景观（Energy Landscape），建立了注意力与反向扩散过程的数学联系。

Result: 研究发现：1. 单个注意力步骤本质上是核加权的后验均值计算；2. 深度和注意力残差在推理中具有不同的统计功能，深度用于细化经验分布，跳跃连接用于后验推断；3. 在特定假设下，该模型能够实现对贝叶斯最优预测器的恢复，其动力学行为与反向扩散过程高度相似。

Conclusion: 本文从统计学角度为Transformer架构提供了理论基础，揭示了注意力和深度在上下文推理中的本质角色。研究表明，Transformer通过非显式密度建模的采样方式，实现了类扩散模型的后验估计，为理解大规模语言模型的涌现能力提供了重要的统计解释。

Abstract: We study minimal attention-only transformers under all-token corruption and show they admit a two-stage empirical Bayes interpretation. A single attention step computes a kernel-weighted posterior mean with respect to the empirical distribution defined by the context. Depth refines this distribution through particle dynamics (Stage 1), while a long-range skip-connection carries the noisy input as a query for posterior inference (Stage 2), revealing distinct statistical roles for depth and attention residuals. The framework isolates a minimal setting in which the context itself induces a depth-dependent energy landscape governing in-context inference. We show that effective denoising can emerge without an explicit noise schedule: a fixed kernel bandwidth and finite integration horizon suffice, yielding a principled depth-noise relationship. We further establish a posterior-mean recovery guarantee for a class of well-behaved priors, where the empirical estimator converges to the Bayes-optimal predictor under asymptotic conditions. Connecting these dynamics to reverse-diffusion limits, our results provide a statistical interpretation of attention as in-context inference via sample-based posterior estimation, without explicit density modeling.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的ILP求解方法主要分为依赖传统求解器（如SCIP、Gurobi）和基于深度学习的方法。学习型方法往往存在泛化能力差、高度依赖外部求解器的问题，因此作者旨在开发一种无需训练、无需外部求解器的采样框架，以提高求解的通用性、鲁棒性和独立性。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于采样的优化框架：1.利用ILP的线性结构，设计了“局部平衡提议”（Locally-Balanced Proposal）来构建转移核，避免了梯度近似；2.集成了“并行回火”（Parallel Tempering）以处理高度多模态的能量景观；3.引入了“惩罚回火”（Penalty Tempering），通过动态调节约束边界来引导搜索，同时保持可行解区域的目标函数结构。

Result: 实验结果表明：该方法在四个基准测试中均优于SCIP；在200秒的时间预算内，在两个任务上达到或超过了Gurobi的性能；在分布偏移场景下表现出显著优于学习型方法的鲁棒性；且在MIPLIB 2017实例中，无需针对性调整即可与经典求解器竞争。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种无需求解器、无需训练的采样优化框架，证明了基于局部平衡提议和多重温度回火的采样策略在解决ILP问题上具有强大的通用性和鲁棒性，为组合优化提供了一种不依赖传统求解器的新路径。

Abstract: Integer Linear Programming (ILP) serves as a versatile framework for modeling a wide range of combinatorial optimization problems, typically addressed by sophisticated exact solvers or heuristics. While learning-based approaches have recently shown their effectiveness, they suffer from poor generalization to out-of-distribution instances and inherent dependence on external solvers. In this work, we propose a solver-free, sampling-based optimization framework for ILP that directly explores discrete feasible regions without training or external solvers. Exploiting the linear structure of ILP, we employ a Locally-Balanced Proposal to construct a transition kernel, thereby avoiding the gradient approximation. To overcome the highly multimodal nature of ILP energy landscapes, we integrate Parallel Tempering. In addition to standard temperature tempering, we introduce penalty tempering, which modulates constraint barriers while preserving the objective landscape over feasible solutions. Empirically, our method consistently outperforms SCIP across all four benchmarks, matches or exceeds Gurobi on two of four tasks within a 200-second budget, and is substantially more robust to distribution shift than learning-based methods. Furthermore, on MIPLIB 2017 instances, our framework remains competitive with classical solvers without any problem-specific tuning.

</details>


### [266] [Rethinking Post-Training Recipes for Multimodal Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29401)
*Haoxin Liu,Yichen Zhou,Rajat Sen,B. Aditya Prakash,Abhimanyu Das*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PostTime 提出了一种多模态时间序列预测新方法，通过后训练 LLM 来作为“修订器”，利用多模态上下文对时间序列基础模型（TSFM）的初步数值预测进行智能修正，显著提升了预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列基础模型（TSFM）虽然在数值预测方面表现优异，但缺乏处理非数值型多模态上下文的能力，而这些上下文往往是塑造现实世界时间序列轨迹的关键。该研究旨在弥合这一鸿沟，利用 LLM 的多模态理解能力增强 TSFM 的预测表现。

Method: 提出名为 PostTime 的后训练方案，结合了监督微调（SFT）和带有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）；设计了自动生成推理轨迹的方法，教导 LLM 在多模态背景下对 TSFM 提供的数值预测进行有条件的干预（修订、保留或忽略）。

Result: 在 TimesX 多模态预测基准测试中，基于 Gemma-3-4B 和 TimesFM-2.5 的 PostTime 方法显著优于单一的 TSFM、纯 LLM 基线模型以及现有的其他多模态预测方法。

Conclusion: 本研究成功证明了将大型语言模型（LLM）作为多模态上下文引导的修订器，能够显著提升现有时间序列基础模型（TSFM）的预测精度。通过将推理能力与数值预测相结合，PostTime 为处理复杂、多模态驱动的时间序列问题提供了一种高效且可扩展的范式。

Abstract: Time-Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) excel at zero-shot unimodal forecasting using numerical data, but unlike LLMs they cannot consume multimodal, non-numerical context that often shape real-world trajectories. In this work, we bridge this gap and argue for a multimodal time-series forecasting approach that post-trains LLMs to act as context-guided revisors over strong numerical TSFM priors. We introduce PostTime, a post-training recipe combining Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), along with a methodology to generate automated reasoning traces for forecast revisions. PostTime teaches an LLM to generate context-conditioned forecast interventions -- decisions to revise, preserve, or ignore the TSFM prior based on the multimodal context. We evaluate this approach on the TimesX multimodal forecasting benchmark using a Gemma-3-4B LLM and TimesFM-2.5 TSFM, and show that it significantly outperforms standalone TSFMs, LLM-only baselines, and existing multimodal forecasting approaches.

### [267] [Information-Directed Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29405)
*Keru Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了信息导向采样（IDS）框架，通过衡量并利用“离线数据后的残余不确定性”来优化离线到在线强化学习过程，在理论和实验上证明了其比传统方法更高效的探索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线数据虽能降低不确定性，但无法完全消除，仍需通过在线交互进行探索。现有的离线到在线策略往往忽略了如何针对“残余不确定性”进行有目的的探索，因此需要一种更科学的方法来优化在线阶段的探索与利用平衡。

Method: 引入条件互信息 $I(χ;τ_{1:T}\mid\mathcal{D}_N)$ 来量化离线数据集之后的残余不确定性；提出信息导向采样（IDS）策略，通过参数 $η$ 平衡瞬时遗憾与信息增益；并证明了IDS可继承参考汤普森采样策略的后悔界限。

Result: 证明了IDS具备通用离线到在线贝叶斯遗憾界；在贝叶斯线性奖励模型中，IDS表现出优于传统汤普森采样的性能，特别是在存在主导但信息丰富的探测样本时；D4RL实验验证了IDS在离线数据存在偏差或低概率残余不确定性场景下的优势。

Conclusion: 该研究通过信息导向采样（IDS）框架，将离线到在线的强化学习问题转化为有效的信息获取与遗憾（regret）之间的权衡，证明了IDS在处理残余不确定性方面的理论优势和实证有效性，为冷启动后的策略优化提供了更稳健的决策方法。

Abstract: Decision-making from offline datasets typically warm-starts a policy or score model from fixed offline data and then refines it with limited online interaction. Offline data reduces uncertainty, but it does not remove the need for exploration; it changes what remains to be explored. We formalise this residual uncertainty by the conditional mutual information $I(χ;τ_{1:T}\mid\mathcal{D}_N)$ between a learning target $χ$ and the online trajectories after conditioning on the offline dataset. This view leads naturally to information-directed sampling (IDS), a family parameterised by $η\ge 0$ that selects actions by trading off instantaneous regret against information gain. We prove a generic offline-to-online Bayesian regret bound for IDS through a ratio certificate: any information-ratio bound satisfied by a reference Thompson-sampling policy over the same randomised policy class is inherited by IDS. In a known-dynamics Bayesian linear-reward model, the conditional mutual information has a log-determinant form, and vanilla IDS ($η=0$) satisfies $\widetilde O\!\left(Hd\min\left\{\sqrt T,\,T\sqrt{C^\dagger_{β,\mathrm{IDS}_0}(N,T)/N}\right\}\right),$ where the coverage coefficient is tied to the visitation distribution induced by vanilla IDS itself. We also identify a warm-start regime with a dominated but informative probe in which vanilla IDS selects the probe while Thompson sampling never does, giving a constant-factor Bayesian regret separation. Controlled bandit experiments and D4RL offline-to-online RL experiments validate this mechanism: IDS is most beneficial when offline data is informative but leaves biased or low-probability residual uncertainty that targeted online actions can resolve, a regime shared by offline RL, offline black-box optimization, and Bayesian optimization.

### [268] [The Good, the Bad, and the Ugly of Markov Boundary for Tabular Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29411)
*Shu Wan,Abhinav Gorantla,Huan Liu,K. Selçuk Candan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模基准测试揭示了马尔可夫边界在表格数据预测中的“理论优越性”与“实际低效性”之间的矛盾，指出当前的因果发现方法未能有效转化为预测性能，并提出了未来预测导向特征选择的改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管理论上马尔可夫边界是实现特征冗余消除和最优预测的充分条件，但在现代表格数据预测任务中，模型仍倾向于使用全特征集进行训练。研究旨在探讨马尔可夫边界在实际应用中的真实预测价值，以及为什么现有的因果发现与特征选择流水线未能充分利用这一理论优势。

Method: 研究使用了SCM3K（包含3,450个任务的合成结构因果模型基准），涉及40到1000个特征的六种不同SCM家族，并评估了六种不同的回归器。通过比较在“预言机边界”（oracle boundary）与“全特征集”上的预测表现，分析了现有因果发现算法在恢复边界后的实际预测效果，并总结了制约性能的三个关键因素。

Result: 研究发现：1. 限制回归器仅使用预言机边界在特征稀疏的大空间中确实能提升性能；2. 现有的因果发现算法由于计算瓶颈和结构恢复导向，通常无法在实际任务中超越全特征集模型；3. 因果发现中的假阳性和假阴性对预测造成的成本高度不对称，且马尔可夫边界并非实现最优预测的唯一特征集合。

Conclusion: 尽管马尔可夫边界在理论上是特征选择的理想目标，但现有的因果发现算法在实际应用中难以有效地将其转化为预测性能的提升。研究强调，预测导向的特征选择应优先考虑预测误差而非单纯的结构恢复，且模型应学习利用因果结构以实现比单一马尔可夫边界更优的性能。

Abstract: Under standard graphical assumptions, the Markov boundary of a target variable is the smallest set of features that renders every other feature redundant. Once the boundary is observed, the target is conditionally independent of the rest of the table. This is a tempting object for tabular prediction, since it names exactly the columns a model should need. Yet modern regressors are still trained on the full feature set. We ask whether the Markov boundary is genuinely useful for prediction on SCM3K, a 3,450-task synthetic SCM benchmark with feature counts from 40 to 1000 and six SCM families, evaluated with six regressors. The answer is more nuanced than the theory suggests. Restricting a regressor to the oracle boundary often improves prediction substantially, and the improvement grows as the feature space becomes larger and sparser. But the natural pipeline of recovering the boundary with causal discovery and training on the recovered mask does not deliver. Existing estimators exhaust the compute budget before reaching the regime where the boundary helps most, and even where they run they rarely beat the full feature set. We trace this to three causes. Discovery optimizes structural recovery rather than prediction. False negatives and false positives carry sharply asymmetric predictive cost. The exact boundary is only one of many feature sets that beat all features. We then develop what these facts imply for prediction-aligned feature selection and for tabular models that learn to use causal structure.

</details>


### [269] [How Much Is a Dataset Worth? Scaling Laws, the Vendi Score, and Matrix Spectral Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29448)
*Jeff A. Bilmes,Gantavya Bhatt,Arnav M. Das*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文为数据评估建立了矩阵谱函数这一统一数学框架，通过开发高效的优化算法，使在大规模数据集上进行数据价值评估成为可能，并经实证发现Facility Location是目前最有效的评估指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的神经缩放定律侧重于数据集大小，而Vendi Score利用量子熵度量数据价值，两者缺乏统一的数学框架。此外，现有数据评估方法在处理大规模数据集时计算成本过高，且尚不清楚何种目标函数能最准确地评估训练子集对下游模型性能的贡献。

Method: 1. 建立理论框架：证明神经缩放定律目标和Vendi Score属于次模函数（submodular），并将Vendi Score归纳为矩阵谱函数（matrix spectral functions）的特例。
2. 算法优化：引入弱矩阵单调函数，并开发基于久期方程（secular-equation）的优化算法，避免了贪婪搜索中重复的特征值分解，将评估效率提升了约35,000倍。
3. 实验对比：在ImageNet-1K等规模数据集上，对比了Vendi Score、DPP、Facility Location及多种矩阵谱变体的评估表现。

Result: 1. 成功将Vendi Score及多种评估目标统一在矩阵谱函数框架下。
2. 通过算法优化，实现了在大规模数据集上直接进行子集选择的性能评估。
3. 实证结果表明，Facility Location在评估数据价值方面优于Vendi Score和DPP。
4. 揭示了现有数据价值评估指标在极端值下的局限性，并证实了数据价值受多种因素影响，不能仅靠基础属性推断。

Conclusion: 研究表明，数据评估不能仅依赖数据量、类别平衡或训练预算等简单指标。尽管Vendi Score在特定范围内具有预测价值，但过度优化可能会导致其预测失效。实验发现Facility Location目标函数在预测子集性能方面表现最优，且随机采样在很多情况下表现出惊人的稳健性。

Abstract: Neural scaling laws appraise data through dataset size, while the Vendi Score uses quantum entropy to measure dataset value. We show both that common neural-scaling-law objectives and the Vendi Score are submodular. We further show that the Vendi Score is a special case of a broader class of submodular objectives that we call matrix spectral functions. This also includes determinantal (DPP) objectives, as well as many others. We also introduce weakly matrix monotone functions and show how they lead to weakly submodular matrix spectral functions, yielding a broad family of practical objectives for data appraisal. We develop secular-equation-based updates that avoid repeated eigendecompositions during greedy optimization, reducing marginal-gain evaluation for $m$-dimensional embeddings by an $O(m)$ factor relative to oracle queries. This yields an average empirical speedup of about 35,000x, making direct optimization of the Vendi Score feasible on ImageNet-1K-scale datasets. Thus enabled, we compare how well several objectives predict the value of training subsets for held-out test performance under fixed-size, class-balanced, and fixed training-budget regimes, including the Vendi Score, DPPs, facility location, and three new matrix spectral variants. Across multiple datasets, facility location performs the best. Direct optimization also reveals that, while the Vendi Score is predictive over moderate score ranges, pushing the objective to higher values can make it a poor downstream performance proxy. We also find that uniformly at random fixed-size subsets, both unconstrained and class-balanced, are remarkably concentrated in both appraisal scores and held-out performance. Finally, we show that size, class balance, and training budget do not alone determine data value: even when controlling for these factors, performance ranges smoothly from good to bad.

Abstract: Representation learning on dynamic graphs requires capturing complex dependencies that evolve across both time and structure. Existing approaches typically adopt fixed temporal decay schemes or predetermined structural propagation depths, limiting their ability to generalize across graphs with diverse interaction frequencies and topological characteristics. We propose Dual-Scale Retentive Dynamics (DSRD), a unified framework that maintains a retentive representation state encoding both temporal memory and structural context. DSRD introduces two key components: (i) a retentive state with dual-scale adaptation that jointly models temporal dynamics and structural propagation within a single recurrent formulation, and (ii) adaptive decay kernels with learnable time-sensitivity parameters that automatically balance short-term responsiveness and long-term retention based on the underlying interaction patterns. We provide theoretical analysis establishing the equivalence between event-wise parallel aggregation and efficient recurrent state updates, as well as stability and boundedness guarantees for the learned dynamics. Extensive experiments on 14 real-world benchmarks demonstrate that DSRD consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance on both link prediction and node classification tasks, with strong generalization across transductive and inductive settings.

To bridge this gap and provide actionable insights, we introduce a comprehensive evaluation framework that systematically characterizes privacy risks across the entire machine learning pipeline, spanning data, architectures, algorithms, and post-training modules. ### [272] [Composing Non-Conjugate Factor Graphs with Closed-Form Variational Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29467)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深层概率架构通常会导致推理过程失去闭式解，从而增加计算复杂度和不确定性量化的难度。研究旨在探索如何通过构建特定的模块，在保证模型深度扩展的同时，保留闭式变分推断的特性。

Method: 识别出五种核心因子图原语（双线性因子、指数链接、Gamma先验、高斯似然和等式节点），并证明由这些原语组成的模型在均值场变分推断下能保持闭式求解。对于非共轭的指数链接，利用高斯矩生成函数和Gamma分布的充分统计量保持了可处理性。

Result: 证明了该构建方式支持从静态集成到动态路由的复杂架构，实现了具有闭式推断的通用函数逼近；在时间序列预测实验中，该框架在不依赖显式学习门控函数的情况下，实现了高效、经过校准的专家混合模型推理。

Conclusion: 该研究通过数学证明确立了一套闭式推理的构建块，成功打破了深层概率模型通常难以进行闭式推断的限制，并展示了其在通用函数逼近和贝叶斯时间序列预测中的有效性。

Abstract: Stacking probabilistic building blocks into deeper architectures typically breaks closed-form inference. We show that closed-form inference can be preserved. We identify five factor-graph primitives: a bilinear factor, an exponential link, a Gamma prior, a Gaussian likelihood, and an equality node, and prove that any model composed from them admits closed-form variational message passing. The construction works because each primitive preserves a small set of message families: under mean-field factorization, messages on Gaussian variables remain Gaussian and messages on precision variables remain Gamma, while the only non-conjugate interface, the exponential link, remains tractable through the Gaussian moment-generating function and the sufficient statistics of the Gamma family. We demonstrate composition at increasing depth, from static ensembles through input-dependent gating to split-branch routing, and show that stacking routing layers encodes arbitrary decision trees, establishing universal function approximation with closed-form inference. Applied to ensemble time-series forecasting, the framework yields a Bayesian mixture of experts in which gating functions are inferred rather than learned, providing calibrated uncertainty over expert selection across five benchmark datasets.

</details>


### [273] [Access Sets Matter: Budgeting Expert Reads for Scalable Weight-Space Model Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29489)
*Yuanyi Wang,Yanggan Gu,Su Lu,Yifan Yang,Zhaoyi Yan,Congkai Xie,Jianmin Wu,Hongxia Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MergePipe 是一种针对大规模语言模型（LLM）的预算感知权重合并框架，通过智能调度专家权重访问计划，在显著降低 I/O 开销和提升计算速度的同时，保证了模型合并的精度与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 LLM 规模下，现有的权重空间合并方法受限于专家权重读取的 I/O 开销。为了解决大规模模型合并中计算资源与存储读取瓶颈的矛盾，需要一种能够在预算约束下高效执行合并操作的系统框架。

Method: 本文提出 MergePipe，一种预算感知的权重合并执行层。其核心方法包括：1. 将 LLM 合并问题建模为“专家访问集”问题；2. 对参数块进行索引；3. 构建确定性的执行计划，根据给定的 I/O 预算决定需要读取的专家增量块；4. 通过可重现的清单（Manifests）执行合并。对于加性合并算子，该方法具备理论上的误差界限。

Result: 在 Qwen 和 Llama 模型合并任务中，MergePipe 将专家读取 I/O 减少了一个数量级，实现了高达 11 倍的加速。实验表明，在预算受限情况下，参数偏离度极低（$O(10^{-3})$），且下游任务性能未出现单调性下降。

Conclusion: MergePipe 证明了在大型语言模型（LLM）权重合并任务中，通过引入预算感知机制，可以在显著降低 I/O 开销的同时，保持极高的模型性能。该研究成功将权重合并范式从纯代数运算转向了资源受限的专家访问优化，为大规模模型的高效整合提供了新的工程路径。

Abstract: Weight-space model merging is usually formulated as an algebraic operation on checkpoints, yet at LLM scale the limiting resource is often the set of expert weights that must be read. We introduce MergePipe, a budget-aware execution layer that casts LLM merging as an \emph{expert access-set} problem: given a merge operator and a checkpoint family in a shared weight coordinate system, choose which expert delta blocks to access under an explicit I/O budget. MergePipe indexes parameter blocks, builds deterministic access plans, and executes the induced budgeted merge with replayable manifests. The plan is budget-sound by construction and recovers the full-read merge at full budget; for fixed-coefficient additive operators, the omitted-update error is bounded by the norm of omitted deltas. Across Qwen and Llama merging workloads, MergePipe reduces expert-read I/O by up to an order of magnitude and achieves up to $11\times$ speedups. Representative budget sweeps show $O(10^{-3})$ parameter deviation from full-read merges and no monotonic degradation on downstream benchmarks.

### [274] [On-Policy Replay for Continual Supervised Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29495)
*Yan Chen,Taojie Zhu,Meng Zhang,Xin Chen,Jiaqi Huang,Dongyang Xu,Yizhi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型持续微调中的灾难性遗忘问题，本文提出了一种名为 OPR（在线策略重放）的简单方法。该方法通过重放模型自身生成的经过奖励过滤的高质量数据，而非依赖复杂的蒸馏技术，显著提升了模型在持续学习任务中的性能保持能力，同时简化了训练流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在进行持续监督微调时，往往会面临“灾难性遗忘”问题，即丧失先前任务的能力。现有的基于在线策略的缓解方法通常需要引入额外的教师模型、辅助损失函数或复杂的蒸馏过程，这些方法往往对训练计划敏感，且容易导致风格漂移。因此，作者旨在寻找一种无需教师模型、无额外损失函数且更简单的在线策略缓解机制。

Method: 作者提出了“在线策略重放”（On-Policy Replay, OPR）方法。该方法不引入额外的辅助损失函数或教师模型，而是通过利用最新的模型检查点在历史提示词上生成响应，并根据任务奖励对生成的响应进行过滤，将表现优异的 (提示词, 模型输出) 对作为常规监督微调（SFT）样本进行重放。该方法通过数据源的策略更新来实现知识的保留，而非传统的模型蒸馏。

Result: 在三个主流指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, Qwen3-8B, Llama3.1-8B-Instruct）及 TRACE 持续学习基准测试中，OPR 表现优异。在极端测试条件下，OPR 将逆向传递（BWT）性能指标从 -13.93 显著提升至 -0.65（10% 重放预算），在所有骨干模型上均实现了 42% 至 46% 的遗忘程度（|BWT|）缩减，且优于基准的 Vanilla Replay 方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种简洁高效的持续学习方法 OPR，通过利用模型自身的输出分布作为监督信号，而非依赖复杂的蒸馏目标或教师模型，有效地缓解了 LLM 在持续监督微调过程中的灾难性遗忘问题。OPR 证明了基于模型当前策略的数据重放比单纯的静态数据重放更具优势，且具有更好的实现简便性和性能表现。

Abstract: Continual supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is the de facto recipe for adapting large language models (LLMs) to a stream of downstream tasks, but it suffers from catastrophic forgetting of earlier capabilities. Recent work shows that on-policy signals -- training on the model's own outputs -- reduce forgetting more reliably than off-policy supervision. Existing on-policy methods route this signal through a new training objective (e.g., self-distillation losses with a teacher copy), inheriting an extra forward pass, schedule sensitivity, and stylistic drift from the teacher.We instead route the on-policy signal through the training data source. Our method, On-Policy Replay (OPR), rolls out the most recent checkpoint on a small budget of historical prompts, filters the generations by a task reward, and replays the surviving (prompt, model response) pairs as ordinary SFT examples. There is no teacher, no auxiliary loss, and no on-the-fly distillation. Across three 7--8B instruction-tuned backbones (Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, Qwen3-8B, Llama3.1-8B-Instruct) on the TRACE continual-learning benchmark, OPR consistently reduces forgetting; on the sharpest stress test (Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, Sequential SFT BWT -13.93), OPR lifts BWT to -0.65 at a 10% replay budget and to -2.29 at a 1% budget -- a 46% reduction in |BWT| over a tuned Vanilla Replay baseline, with 42--46% reductions observed across all three backbones. We give a KL-shrinkage interpretation that places OPR and prior on-policy distillation methods on a single axis, and we present a counterintuitive finding that explains why Vanilla Replay is already a strong baseline: low-score replay is uniformly worse than Vanilla Replay, demonstrating that the active ingredient in OPR is the on-policy distribution, not the response quality alone.Our code is available at https://github.com/Yancey2024/OnPolicyReplay.

</details>


### [275] [Quotient DAGs for Off-Policy Evaluation:Forward-Flow Importance Sampling and Exact Slate Propensities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29500)
*Ziwen Xie,Shaowen Xiang,Hongyu He,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对离线策略评估中因处理无关序列信息导致的方差和计算难题，提出了一种基于商DAG和动态规划的高效计算框架，实现了无序推荐列表的精确倾向评分估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离线策略评估（OPE）中，标准的加权重要性采样方法常将数据生成过程中的无关细节（如推荐列表的顺序）视为重要信息，导致由于“干扰方差”而产生的估算偏差及巨大的计算开销（特别是在自回归式推荐系统中需要进行阶乘级枚举）。本文旨在解决这一计算与统计效率问题。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于“商DAG（Quotient-DAG）”的框架，将对评估结果无影响的历史轨迹进行合并。在针对组合推荐的特定场景中，利用目标策略与行为策略之间的前向流比率（Forward-flow ratios），通过动态规划算法（Forward-DP）在子集DAG上直接计算精确的无序倾向评分，从而绕过了对所有排列顺序进行求和的计算开销。

Result: 实验表明，该方法能够有效地在自回归式推荐系统下计算精确的无序倾向评分，显著降低了计算复杂度，使得在上下文相关环境下进行更准确的策略评估和模型选择成为可能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“商DAG”视角和Forward-DP算法，为自回归式推荐系统等存在冗余序列信息的场景，提供了一种高效、精确的离线策略评估方法，避免了昂贵的阶乘级计算，提升了离线评估的实用性。

Abstract: Off-policy evaluation estimates how a target policy would perform using data collected by a different behavior policy, which is crucial when online testing is costly or risky, such as in recommendation or healthcare. Standard importance sampling reweights each logged trajectory, but it can treat details of the generation process as meaningful even when the evaluation target ignores them: for example, an autoregressive slate recommender may generate an ordered sequence of items while the reward and downstream estimator depend only on the unordered slate. This creates nuisance variance and a computational gap, since exact unordered slate propensities require summing over all generation orders. We introduce a quotient-DAG view that merges histories equivalent for evaluation and assigns weights using target-to-behavior forward-flow ratios on the merged graph. For slate recommendation under a set-sufficient next-item interface, this yields Forward-DP, a subset-DAG dynamic program that computes exact unordered propensities without factorial enumeration. The resulting propensity primitive enables practical propensity-based evaluation and model selection for context-dependent autoregressive slate loggers.

Result: 测试结果显示，即使是当前最强大的大模型在进行细粒度金融诊断和表现拒答行为时也表现不佳。在所有被评估模型中，“合理拒答”是性能表现最薄弱的环节。通过针对性微调 8B 模型，可以在该基准上获得与前沿模型竞争的性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，尽管大模型在处理韩国金融领域的多轮检索增强生成任务上有所进展，但在处理细粒度的金融诊断和“合理拒答”（justified abstention）方面仍存在显著局限。微调较小参数模型可在特定任务上达到与前沿模型相当的性能，但整体而言，模型在识别复杂幻觉和进行准确拒答方面仍有很大提升空间。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have advanced financial automation through Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), yet hallucinations remain a critical barrier to deployment in high-stakes environments. We introduce K-FinHallu, the first benchmark for hallucination detection in multi-turn Korean financial RAG. Benchmarking frontier and open-source LLMs as hallucination detectors, we find that even the strongest models struggle with fine-grained financial diagnostics and refusal behavior. While fine-tuning an 8B model on our training split yields performance competitive with frontier LLMs, justified abstention remains the weakest axis across all evaluated models.

### [277] [AsymVLM: Asymmetric Token Pruning for Efficient Vision-Language Model Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29535)
*Yilin Feng,Ahmed Burak Gulhan,Mahmut Taylan Kandemir*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AsymVLM 针对视觉语言模型中视觉与文本模态的不同特性（空间冗余 vs. 因果依赖），通过差异化的剪枝与剔除策略，在显著降低计算成本的同时提升了推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有压缩方法对视觉和文本模态采取统一处理，忽略了两者本质上的差异：视觉 tokens 存在空间冗余且主导预填充阶段，而文本 tokens 具有因果依赖且在解码阶段不断累积。作者旨在利用这种非对称特性，优化视觉语言模型的推理效率。

Method: 提出了 AsymVLM 模型，采取非对称压缩策略：1. 在预填充（prefill）阶段，利用学习到的重要性评分器对具有空间冗余性的视觉 tokens 进行激进剪枝，并采用自适应预算分配；2. 在解码（decoding）阶段，针对具有因果依赖性的文本 tokens，采用基于时间阈值的剔除策略，仅在超出固定预算时执行。

Result: 实验表明，AsymVLM 在实现最高达 54% 的 FLOPs 节省的同时，在文档和图表理解任务上比现有方法提升了 2-3% 的准确率，并在整体基准测试中保持竞争力；在文本密集场景下，其缓存剔除策略显著优于传统 LLM 压缩方法。

Conclusion: AsymVLM 通过针对视觉和文本模态特性设计差异化的压缩策略，有效解决了视觉语言模型在推理过程中的计算瓶颈问题，在大幅降低计算开销的同时提升了特定任务的准确性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) process thousands of visual tokens per image alongside comparatively few text tokens, yet existing compression methods treat both modalities uniformly. We observe that the two modalities have fundamentally different properties: vision tokens are spatially redundant and dominate prefill, while text tokens are causally dependent and accumulate during decoding. Based on this asymmetry, we propose and empirically evaluate AsymVLM, which applies aggressive pruning to vision tokens before prefill using a learned importance scorer with per-sample adaptive budgeting, and temporal threshold-based eviction to text tokens only when they exceed a fixed budget. Our experiments indicate that AsymVLM achieves the highest FLOPs savings (up to 54%) among state-of-the-art methods while outperforming existing approaches by 2--3% on document and chart understanding tasks where visual information is spatially localized and query-specific, and maintaining competitive accuracy on holistic benchmarks. In text-dominated scenarios, our eviction strategy substantially outperforms standard LLM cache compression methods by adapting to the short-context nature of VLM.

### [278] [Singularity-aware Optimization via Randomized Geometric Probing: Towards Stable Non-smooth Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29547)
*Ruoran Xu,Borong She,Xiaobo Jin,Qiufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对深度学习中 ReLU 等非光滑组件引起的梯度振荡问题，本文提出了 S-Adam 优化器，通过引入局部几何不稳定性（LGI）指标进行动态步长调节，显著提升了模型在非光滑训练场景下的收敛性和泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代深度学习模型中 ReLU 等非光滑组件导致损失地形不平滑，使得 Adam 等自适应优化器在 Clarke 次微分区域产生剧烈的“梯度颤动”（gradient chattering），进而导致收敛困难和泛化能力下降。

Method: 提出了一种名为“奇异感知 Adam”（S-Adam）的优化器。核心在于设计了“局部几何不稳定性”（LGI）指标，通过随机方向导数的方差来估计 Clarke 次微分的直径，并引入了基于该指标的自适应阻尼机制（exp(-λρ)），在高度不稳定的区域动态减小更新步长。

Result: 在 CIFAR-100 上实现了高达 6% 的准确率提升，在 TinyImageNet 上提升了 3%。实验证明 S-Adam 在量化感知训练（QAT）和高噪声小批量学习中有效抑制了梯度振荡，且收敛速度保持在最优的 O(1/√T)。

Conclusion: S-Adam 成功通过局部几何不稳定性度量（LGI）解决了非光滑优化中的梯度振荡问题，证明了该方法在理论上具有收敛保证，并在实践中显著提升了模型在量化感知训练及高噪声环境下的性能。

Abstract: Deep learning optimization relies heavily on the assumption of smooth loss landscapes, a condition systematically violated by modern architectures due to non-smooth components such as ReLU activations and quantization operators. In such non-smooth regimes, adaptive optimizers such as Adam suffer from gradient chattering, violent oscillations caused by conflicting signals within the Clarke subdifferential, leading to poor convergence and suboptimal generalization. To address this, we introduce Singularity-aware Adam (S-Adam), a novel optimizer that stabilizes training by dynamically modulating step sizes based on local geometric instability. Our key contribution is the Local Geometric Instability (LGI) metric, a computationally efficient estimator of the Clarke subdifferential diameter derived from the variance of randomized directional derivatives. S-Adam incorporates an adaptive damping mechanism exp(-$λ$$ρ$) that decelerates updates in high-instability regions while preserving fast convergence in smooth basins. We provide a rigorous convergence analysis using differential inclusions, proving that S-Adam converges almost surely to ($δ$,$ε$)-Clarke stationary points at the optimal O(1/$\sqrt(T)$) rate. Empirical evaluations on Quantization-Aware Training (QAT) and high-noise small-batch learning demonstrate that S-Adam consistently outperforms AdamW and Prox-SGD, achieving accuracy gains of up to 6 percent on CIFAR-100 and 3 percent on TinyImageNet while effectively mitigating gradient oscillations.

</details>


### [279] [Why Larger Models Learn More: Effects of Capacity, Interference, and Rare-Task Retention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29548)
*Jing Huang,Daniel Wurgaft,Rachit Bansal,Laura Ruis,Naomi Saphra,David Alvarez-Melis,Andrew Kyle Lampinen,Christopher Potts,Ekdeep Singh Lubana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过合成实验和OLMo模型预训练揭示，大模型学习能力更强的原因在于其能缓解不同任务间的资源竞争与梯度干扰，从而让模型不仅能处理高频简单任务，还能捕获稀有和复杂的任务特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示“为什么模型规模越大，越能学习到小模型无法掌握的任务”这一核心现象背后的深层机制，特别是探究数据分布、资源分配与梯度干扰之间的关系。

Method: 1. 构建现象学论证：基于幂律缩放理论说明大模型在处理特定数据分布时的固有优势；2. 合成数据实验：设计包含不同频率和复杂度任务的混合任务集，观察模型资源分配与学习效果；3. 机制分析：探究资源分配与梯度干扰机制（即常见任务对稀有任务特征的覆盖）；4. 大规模验证：通过不同参数规模（4M-4B）的OLMo模型在受控数据集上的预训练进行实证。

Result: 1. 模型存在“数据诱导的资源竞争”：小模型倾向于将神经元资源集中在简单或高频任务上，导致无法学习稀有或复杂任务；2. 大模型优势在于“减少梯度干扰”：大模型能为高频任务分配足够资源，使其梯度更新变得平缓，从而避免对稀有任务特征的覆盖；3. 实验验证：在OLMo模型上的大规模实验证明，仅大模型能捕捉稀有复杂任务，且其内部表示蕴含更多任务特征，且任务间的梯度干扰显著降低。

Conclusion: 该研究通过数据中心视角解释了模型规模效应的本质：大模型能够通过分配更多资源来减少不同任务间的梯度干扰，从而学习到小模型因资源竞争而无法习得的低频或复杂任务。该结论为模型大小选择及训练数据配比提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Larger models learn tasks smaller models do not. What drives this phenomenon? We develop a simple phenomenological argument that power-law scaling already suggests that a larger model will be able to learn a part of the data distribution that a smaller model fails to learn, even with infinite training data. To validate this claim and identify its causes, we study the effects of model scaling on a synthetic setup consisting of a mixture of tasks that show monotonic scaling curves. The results point to a data-induced competition over resources (neurons). Specifically, smaller models allocate their neurons to high frequency or low complexity tasks, and so they learn solutions that perform poorly on rare and complex tasks. Moreover, this happens even when solutions capable of expressing the desired task exist. We then assess how a larger model circumvents this data-centric bottleneck, finding that it traces to a reduced interference mechanism: larger models can allocate enough resources to common tasks that the gradient updates for those tasks become weak, which means that they do not overwrite rare-task features as they slowly accumulate. Finally, to further validate these claims, we pretrain OLMo models (4M to 4B parameters) on novel tasks of varying frequency and complexity. The results mirror those from our synthetic data experiments: only the larger OLMo models learn the infrequent and complex tasks, and these larger models embed more task features in their representations and show less gradient interference between tasks. Overall, we offer a data-centric account of why larger models learn tasks that smaller models fail to. This helps explain why larger models are better in practice, and it can inform practical questions concerning model sizing and training data mixtures.

</details>


### [280] [On the Construction and Implications of Low-Loss Valleys in LoRA-based Bayesian Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29580)
*Daniel Dold,Emanuel Sommer,Julius Kobialka,Oliver Dürr,David Rügamer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LoRA-Curve，一种通过分段贝塞尔曲线在 LoRA 空间中连接独立最优解的方法，成功解决了现有 LoRA 集成方法中无法跨越损耗屏障的问题，实现了更优的认知不确定性估计与函数多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 LoRA 已成为大语言模型微调的主流，但如何进行有效的认知不确定性估计仍具挑战。现有的离散式集成方法在 LoRA 空间中表现不佳，且尚不明确 LoRA 空间中是否存在类似全参数空间中那样的“低损耗路径（low-loss valleys）”来连接不同最优解，从而实现更好的贝叶斯模型平均。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 LoRA-Curve 的方法，在 LoRA 参数空间内利用分段贝塞尔曲线进行参数化。该方法包含两种配置：一是通过联合优化所有控制点来构建自由曲线，二是通过锚定配置连接独立微调得到的 LoRA 最优解。此外，结合平坦极小值扰动（flat-minima perturbations）和 Jensen-Shannon 散度正则化器，实现了模型在低损耗路径上的函数多样性探索。

Result: 实验表明，在线性插值方法遭遇严重的损耗屏障（loss barriers）时，LoRA-Curve 的锚定多段曲线成功地在独立最优解之间建立了连续的低损耗通路。在 Qwen2.5 7B 模型上的基准测试证明，该方法在不牺牲性能的前提下，显著提高了预测分布的互信息（mutual information），有效地将参数空间的连续遍历与函数多样性关联起来。

Conclusion: LoRA-Curve 通过在低秩适应空间内构建分段贝塞尔曲线，成功连接了独立的 LoRA 最优解，并证明了低损耗路径的存在。该方法不仅在理论上保证了路径连续性和 Lipschitz 正则性，还在实际应用中通过增强函数多样性提升了模型的预测不确定性估计能力，为大规模语言模型的贝叶斯模型平均提供了一种高效且有效的实现方案。

Abstract: While parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods like low-rank adaptation (LoRA) are standard for large language models, principled estimation of epistemic uncertainty remains challenging. Recent results in the LoRA regime suggest that discrete multi-mode approaches such as deep ensembles offer little benefit over single-mode methods. This contradicts broader observations in deep learning, where ensembling independent optima typically improves generalization, and linking these modes through continuous low-loss valleys further enhances Bayesian model averaging (BMA). Whether such structure exists in the LoRA space and whether it yields functional diversity missed by local or discrete methods has not been studied. We introduce LoRA-Curve, a segmented Bézier curve parameterization in the LoRA space, with two variants: a free configuration that jointly optimizes all control points, and an anchored configuration that connects independently fine-tuned LoRA optima. We prove pathwise continuity and Lipschitz regularity of the loss along the curve and empirically show, across reasoning and classification benchmarks with Qwen2.5 7B, that linear interpolation encounters loss barriers, while our anchored multi-segment curves connect independent optima through continuous low-loss valleys. Combined with flat-minima perturbations and a Jensen-Shannon divergence regularizer, LoRA-Curve yields measurably higher mutual information of the predictive distribution without sacrificing performance, and links continuous parameter-space traversal to functional diversity.
