### [326] [ExDBSCAN: Explaining DBSCAN with Counterfactual Reasoning -- Additional Material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30225)
*Pernille Matthews,Lena Krieger,Tommaso Amico,Artur Zimek,Thomas Seidl,Ira Assent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 DBSCAN 聚类算法缺乏可解释性的问题，本文提出了 ExDBSCAN 方法。该方法利用物理模型原理生成多样且贴近数据的反事实解释，为聚类结果提供了清晰、可操作的洞察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚类算法（如 DBSCAN）缺乏直观的可解释性，用户难以理解特定数据点被划分为内点或离群点的具体原因，也无法评估分配结果对数据微小扰动的鲁棒性。现有的监督学习解释方法无法直接迁移至无监督的聚类场景。

Method: 作者提出了 ExDBSCAN，这是一种密度感知型的后验解释方法。该方法构建了一个密度连接加权图，并采用受物理模型启发的优化策略：通过“排斥力”保证反事实解释的多样性，通过“吸引力”确保其与原始数据点的邻近性，同时提供反事实有效性的理论保证。

Result: 在 30 个表格数据集上的实证评估表明，ExDBSCAN 在所有对比基线模型中表现最优，能够生成高质量的解释，并在保持反事实 100% 有效性的同时，实现了极高的多样性和邻近性平衡。

Conclusion: ExDBSCAN 是一个有效的 DBSCAN 后验可解释性框架。它通过物理启发的优化方法，成功地为聚类分配提供了兼具多样性和邻近性的反事实解释，弥补了 DBSCAN 在可解释性方面的空白。

Abstract: Clustering is an unsupervised technique for grouping data points by similarity. While explainability methods exist for supervised machine learning, they are not directly applicable to clustering, making it challenging to understand cluster assignments. This interpretability gap is particularly evident in the popular density-based method DBSCAN, which assigns points as inliers (cluster members in dense regions) or outliers (noise points in sparse regions). DBSCAN does not provide insight into why a particular point receives its assignment or whether its assignment is robust to small changes in the data. To address the lack of explainability, we introduce ExDBSCAN, a density-aware, post-hoc explanation method. ExDBSCAN offers actionable counterfactual explanations, with theoretical guarantees for validity. It generates multiple counterfactuals using a density connected weighted graph, adopting a physics-inspired model that repels counterfactual candidates from one another (diversity), while pulling them toward the instance to explain (proximity). Empirical evaluation on 30 tabular datasets comparing against four baselines shows that ExDBSCAN outperforms all baselines while attaining perfect validity and retrieving diverse, proximal counterfactuals.

### [327] [Anti Mode-Collapse in Mean-Field Transformer via Auxiliary Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30229)
*Masaaki Imaizumi,Masanori Koyama,Noboru Isobe,Kohei Hayashi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文利用平均场Transformer理论研究了模式坍缩问题，发现位置编码和提示词等辅助变量通过防止token分布收敛至单一狄拉克测度，有效解决了长层推理中的坍缩现象，并证明了这些机制具有表示通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的平均场Transformer模型理论分析表明，在长序列推理（多层）中会发生模式坍缩现象（即所有token分布收敛至同一点），这与实际模型表现不符。本研究旨在探讨为何实际模型中引入的位置编码等辅助变量能够打破这种理论上的坍缩，并揭示其背后的动力学机制。

Method: 利用基于平均场（mean-field）的Transformer理论模型，通过分析能量最大化分布的性质，研究token交互行为；引入辅助变量（如位置编码和提示词），并证明其如何通过推后映射（pushforward）机制防止分布坍缩，同时分析这些机制的表示通用性和亚稳态性质，并结合数学实验进行验证。

Result: 研究证明了辅助变量可以作为对抗模式坍缩的反作用力，使得能量最大化分布不再退化为单一点，而是呈现为辅助变量分布的推后映射；此外，论证了位置编码与提示插入在极限条件下具备表示通用性，能够表达广泛的分布类别。

Conclusion: 本研究通过理论分析证实，位置编码和提示插入等辅助变量不仅能有效防止Transformer模型在深层推理中发生模式坍缩（即token分布退化为单一狄拉克测度），还具备理论上的表示通用性，为理解模型架构设计提供了坚实的理论支撑。

Abstract: We use a mean-field-based transformer model to theoretically investigate how auxiliary variables, such as positional encoding, prevent mode collapse of self-attention mechanisms. The use of mean-field transformers to analyze the properties of self-attention mechanisms has garnered significant attention in recent years due to their ability to comprehensively analyze token interactions. However, analysis of this simple model suggests that mode collapse, where token distributions degenerate to a single point, occurs during long inferences (i.e., many layers), indicating a discrepancy with reality. This study investigates this mean-field transformer model and demonstrates that the introduction of auxiliary variables, such as positional encoding, acts as a counterforce against theoretical mode collapse. Specifically, we show that in the theoretical scheme, the energy-maximizing distribution does not degenerate to a single point; instead, it is characterized by a pushforward of the auxiliary variable distribution, thereby avoiding concentration in the Dirac measure. Our main examples are the positional encoding and the fixed prompt insertion treated as a parallel auxiliary-variable mechanism. Furthermore, we demonstrate that positional encoding and prompt insertion possess universality of representation in the limit, meaning that the limit distribution of inference can exactly represent a wide class of distributions. We also analyze several key properties of positional encoding and metastability, and validate our theoretical results through mathematical experiments.

</details>


### [328] [How's it going? Reinforcement learning in language models recruits a functional welfare axis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30232)
*Andy Q Han,David J. Chalmers,Pavel Izmailov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现强化学习并不创造新的内部表征，而是通过招募预训练模型中早已存在的“福利评估”轴线（即衡量目标达成程度的内在维度）来引导模型行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨强化学习（RL）如何改变大型语言模型的内部表征机制，特别是试图揭示RL训练如何将外部奖励信号转化为模型内部的行为引导，以及这种机制是“创造”出来的还是“招募”预存特征的结果。

Method: 研究者在一个语义中立的迷宫环境中对多个语言模型进行强化学习训练，提取出奖励和惩罚轨迹的概念向量。通过跨任务评估、向量对齐分析、控制变量实验（模型架构、训练方法、微调方式等）以及对比监督微调（SFT）和预训练模型，分析这些向量在迷宫之外的泛化能力和行为影响。

Result: 实验表明，惩罚向量表现出负面福利特征（如导致拒绝、不确定性、负面情绪关联），而奖励向量则表现出相反的特征，两者近乎反平行。这些特征在模型训练前以及仅预训练模型中即已存在，且具有高度的鲁棒性，不受训练算法或微调方式的显著干扰。

Conclusion: 研究认为，强化学习并没有在语言模型中创建新的表征，而是招募（recruits）并强化了预训练模型中原本就存在的关于“功能性福利”（functional welfare，即关于系统目标达成程度的评估）的轴线。这种机制解释了简单的奖励信号如何能够广泛地改变模型行为，对模型的可解释性、对齐技术及训练动态具有深远意义。

Abstract: How does reinforcement learning shape a language model's internal representations? We present evidence that RL recruits a pre-existing representation of functional welfare: an estimate of how well or badly the system is doing, relative to its goals. We train several language models in a novel, semantically neutral maze environment. We then extract concept vectors for rewarded and punished trajectories, and evaluate those vectors in settings unrelated to the maze environment. The punishment vector behaves like a representation of negative welfare: it promotes failure and impossibility tokens, it aligns with negative emotion concepts, it negatively tracks goal-achievement, and steering with it induces negative self-reports, pathological backtracking, refusal, and uncertainty. The positive reward vector behaves as the mirror image, and the two are nearly antiparallel. These effects are robust when controlling for tile-to-reward mapping, scale, instruct tuning, RL training algorithm, model family, and LoRA versus full-finetuning, and largely persist when we replace RL with supervised fine-tuning. Importantly, the vectors are effective in models before they have undergone maze training. Combined with observations that the effects also appear in pretrain-only models, we therefore argue that this functional welfare axis pre-exists post-training: it is recruited, rather than created, by post-training. While we make no claims about any experience of welfare, the axis offers a demonstration that minimal reward signals can broadly affect model behavior by recruiting pre-existing welfare-like representations, with implications for interpretability, post-training dynamics, and alignment.

</details>


### [329] [Statistical Embeddings for Similarity, Retrieval, and Interpretable Alignment of Numeric Tabular Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30289)
*M. Ross Kunz,John Merickel,Keith Wilson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用EDA描述符和规范相关分析（CCA）处理异构数值数据的新框架，实现了跨数据集的高精度检索与特征对齐，同时支持差分隐私，为大语言模型融入科研数据提供了可解释且安全的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在处理异构数值型表格数据时缺乏原生机制，现有的方法要么局限于单一数据集的预测建模，要么在跨数据集对齐上缺乏可解释性，无法有效处理不同变量定义和特征约定的数据集。

Method: 1. 使用结构化探索性数据分析（EDA）描述符提取数值型数据集的特征；2. 利用预训练的句子转换器（Sentence Transformer）将描述符嵌入至共享向量空间；3. 采用规范相关分析（CCA）量化数据集间的相似度；4. 引入惩罚项（Penalized CCA）以识别驱动对齐的关键变量，实现可解释的映射；5. 在嵌入前可选地应用差分隐私技术，确保数据隐私与安全性。

Result: 在包含15个通用基准、材料信息学和核级石墨表征等领域的数据集测试中，该方法达到了0.9的P@1得分。实验证明，其在嵌入消融和不同差分隐私预算下仍表现出稳健的最近邻检索能力和聚类结构。

Conclusion: 该研究通过探索性数据分析（EDA）描述符和规范相关分析（CCA）的结合，成功构建了一种跨异构数值型数据集的有效对齐框架。该方法不仅实现了高精度的相似性检索，还通过稀疏化技术保证了模型的可解释性，为将复杂的数值数据集成到大语言模型（如RAG流水线）中提供了稳健的科学范式。

Abstract: Numeric tabular datasets are the dominant data format in scientific practice, yet large language models lack native mechanisms for representing numeric datasets in a meaningful way across heterogeneous feature spaces. Existing approaches either target predictive modeling over individual datasets, which requires a shared set of variable definitions, or lack mechanisms for interpretable cross-dataset alignment. The proposed methodology characterizes numeric tabular datasets through structured exploratory data analysis descriptors, embeds those descriptors into a shared vector space using a pretrained sentence transformer, and quantifies cross-dataset similarity via Canonical Correlation Analysis (CCA). Furthermore, a penalized formulation of CCA is applied to recover sparse, interpretable variable-level correspondences between datasets, identifying which statistical descriptors or variable-level quantities drive cross-dataset alignment without requiring shared variable names or feature conventions. Differential privacy is optionally applied to the descriptor set prior to embedding, supporting deployment in sensitive data contexts without requiring access to raw observations at time of comparison. The methodology is evaluated across 15 datasets spanning general-purpose benchmarks, materials informatics, and nuclear-grade graphite characterization. Results demonstrate a total P@1 score of 0.9, with known nearest-neighbor retrieval and cluster structure remaining robust across embedding ablations and differential privacy budgets. The proposed framework provides a principled pathway for integrating heterogeneous numeric data into retrieval-augmented generation pipelines while preserving statistical context, with direct applications to data-driven algorithm selection and simulation model initialization for unknown datasets.

### [330] [Self-Trained Verification for Training- and Test-Time Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30290)
*Chen Henry Wu,Aditi Raghunathan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对推理模型自我提升过程中验证器能力不足的难题，本文提出STV方法，通过利用参考解作为监督信号训练验证器，并将其集成到训练循环（ViL）中，实现了推理性能的显著跃升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理模型的自我提升受限于验证器性能瓶颈：测试时的验证-细化循环（V-R loop）因验证器得分膨胀或反馈泛化而失效，训练时的自训练因引入低质量数据而失败。核心问题在于缺乏高质量的错误检测训练信号。

Method: 1. 自训练验证（STV）：通过让模型观察参考解来学习识别自身生成的错误，从而训练一个更强大的验证器。2. 验证器闭环训练（ViL）：在推理训练过程中引入STV验证器的反馈，通过强化学习进一步优化生成器。

Result: 1. 测试时：STV在数学推理任务上将准确率提升约2倍，在科学推理任务上提升了14倍（从1.5%到21%）。2. 训练时：ViL方法在RL收敛的基础上进一步提升了33%的pass@1准确率；且模型在测试时不依赖验证器时，其独立推理能力也比标准RL提升了30%。

Conclusion: 通过将“在提供参考答案时能发现错误”这一不对称性转化为监督目标，本文提出的STV框架显著提升了模型在推理任务中的验证能力，并证明了将验证过程内嵌于训练循环（ViL）中可以进一步突破传统强化学习（RL）的性能上限，为推理模型的大规模自我提升指明了新方向。

Abstract: Self-improvement at scale has been a longstanding goal for reasoning models, and there are two natural places to do it: at test time, through verification-refinement (V-R) loops; and at training time, through self-training methods. Both are gated by the same bottleneck: the verifier. V-R loops stall when verifier scores inflate while accuracy stagnates, and when feedback is too generic to act on; self-training fails similarly when bad self-generated data are added to training. Better verification would unlock both, but the capability we want to train, i.e., catching self-generated errors, lacks training signal. To address this challenge, we propose self-trained verification (STV). Our key observation is that, while a model cannot catch these errors alone, it can when shown the reference solution. We turn this asymmetry into a supervision target and train the verifier to imitate a more informed version of itself. At test time, STV substantially improves V-R loops on hard problems, while alternatives (e.g., SFT, RL on verifier scores, and even meta-verifiers) do not. STV roughly doubles accuracy on hard math and lifts it 14x on scientific reasoning tasks (1.5% to 21%). At training time, we additionally train the generator using RL with STV verifier's feedback inside the V-R loop - a procedure we call verifier-in-the-loop training (ViL). Starting from an RL-converged generator, ViL yields a further 33% gain in pass@1. More notably, the generator's standalone pass@1, with no verifier at test time, climbs 30% relative past where standard RL had converged. Hence, the next frontier in reasoning on hard problems may lie in how we train for and with verification.

*Zhenyu Sun,Zheng Xu,Ermin Wei*

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) typically relies on static reward models to align Large Language Models with human preferences. However, human values are inherently diverse and heterogeneous, and a single reward model often lacks the robustness required to generalize to unseen preference domains. While existing multi-reward frameworks attempt to address this, they are often restricted to a fixed set of known domains and fail to adapt to unseen human distributions without costly retraining. In this work, we propose In-Context Reward Adaptation, a transformer-based framework designed to model diverse and unseen human preferences on the fly. By leveraging the in-context learning capabilities of transformers, our approach adaptively infers the underlying reward structure from a small set of preference demonstrations. We demonstrate that while a standard transformer architecture is insufficient for this task by characterizing an asymptotic bias to the ground-truth, incorporating human response time as an auxiliary input signal enables the model to successfully adapt to preferences from previously unseen domains. Our findings show that this approach provides a more robust foundation for preference modeling, allowing for the representation of heterogeneous rewards and preference distribution shift, and offering a scalable path toward more flexible human-AI alignment.

### [332] [SoundnessBench: Can Your AI Scientist Really Tell Good Research Ideas from Bad Ones?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30329)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者构建了SoundnessBench基准测试，包含1,099个从ICLR论文投稿重构的机器学习研究建议，并配有同行评审的严谨性（soundness）评分。作者在12个前沿大模型上进行了评估，对比了不同提示词策略（标准提示 vs. 激进提示），并排除了公共语料库污染、论文识别短语、表面特征及人类审计质量等混杂因素的影响。

Result: 实验发现大模型在评估科研建议时存在普遍的“乐观偏差”：标准提示下，模型容易将低严谨性的建议误判为严谨；而采用激进提示后，错误则从假阳性大量转化为假阴性。这些表现无法通过单一的混杂因素解释，证实了模型在该任务上的鲁棒性不足。

Conclusion: 当前的大型语言模型在评估科研想法的“严谨性”方面尚不可靠，无法作为独立的科学评审“首道关卡”。研究指出模型存在普遍的乐观偏差，且单纯通过提示词工程难以在假阳性和假阴性之间取得平衡。未来需要更深入的研究来解决评估偏差问题，以真正实现科研自动化。

Abstract: Autonomous AI research agents aim to accelerate scientific discovery by automating the research pipeline, from hypothesis generation to peer review. However, existing benchmarks rarely test a fundamental bottleneck: whether Large Language Models can judge the methodological viability of a research idea before expending time and computational resources. We introduce SoundnessBench, a curated benchmark of 1,099 machine-learning research proposals reconstructed from ICLR submissions, labeled with reviewer soundness sub-scores, and audited against source papers. SoundnessBench should be interpreted as a benchmark for recoverable proposal-stage soundness rather than exact prediction of full-paper review outcomes. Across 12 frontier LLMs, we find a pervasive optimism bias: under standard prompting, models frequently rate low-soundness proposals as sound, while aggressive prompting largely shifts errors from false positives to false negatives. Additional controls for public-corpus contamination, paper-identifying phrases, surface features, and human audit quality suggest that this behavior is not explained by a single confounder. Our results indicate that current LLMs are not yet reliable as standalone first-gate evaluators for scientific rigor.

### [333] [When, why, and how do diffusion posterior samplers fail? A finite-sample lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30330)
*Benjamin A. Burns,Sara Fridovich-Keil*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种有限样本视角来分析扩散模型在逆问题采样中的误差，指出中间时刻似然近似的不精确会导致后验偏差和幻觉，并提供了一个通用的诊断框架来评估后验采样器的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型在成像逆问题的后验采样中表现出色，但其在推理阶段对似然函数使用不精确的近似处理，缺乏深入的理论解释。现有方法在中间时间步长的近似对最终采样后验分布的影响尚不明确，常导致难以解释的失败案例，如幻觉产生或对特定参数过于敏感。因此，需要从理论上阐明这些近似是如何引发错误的。

Method: 作者引入了一种“有限样本视角”（finite-sample perspective）的后验采样分析方法。通过将后验近似推演至训练集规模趋于无穷大的极限情况，该方法能够对任意正向模型和先验分布进行任意精度的分析。该方法作为一种诊断工具，不依赖于特定的似然近似技术或模型类型（线性或非线性），从而评估采样过程在中间时刻的偏差。

Result: 研究发现：1. 主流后验采样方法在中间时间步长往往会高估或低估后验分布的散度；2. 这种不准确会导致对提前停止（early stopping）的敏感性增加、后验模态权重计算错误，以及产生与真实后验不符的幻觉；3. 即使在简单的线性测量模型下，只要先验分布是多模态的，且采样过程中中间分布的散度估计不准确，就会产生上述错误。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了现有扩散模型在逆问题后验采样中，由于中间时刻似然近似不精确，会导致后验分布偏差、模态权重错误及幻觉现象。通过有限样本视角，研究者证明了这些错误即使在简单线性模型中也会因先验分布的多模态性质而产生。本研究所提出的框架为诊断和评估后验采样算法的准确性提供了通用的理论支撑。

Abstract: Diffusion models have excellent capacity to model complex distributions of natural data, which has made them a popular and effective choice for posterior sampling in imaging inverse problems. Existing methods can incorporate any measurement model at inference time but must use an inexact approximation for the likelihood at intermediate timesteps for computational tractability. Although these approximations can often work well empirically, their downstream effect on the sampled posterior is poorly understood and can result in unexplained failures. To understand when, why, and how these likelihood approximations propagate to erroneous posterior distributions, we introduce a finite-sample perspective on posterior sampling that approximates the posterior to arbitrary precision as training set size tends towards infinity, for any forward model and prior distribution. Using this finite-sample lens, we observe that popular posterior sampling approximations tend to under- or over-estimate the spread of the posterior at intermediate timesteps, causing downstream consequences including sensitivity to early stopping time, inaccurate relative weighting of posterior modes, and hallucination, both of prior modes that are not in the posterior and likelihood modes that are not supported by the prior. Moreover, we find that the cause of these posterior errors requires neither a nonlinear measurement model nor a multimodal posterior, but can arise solely due to a multimodal prior and inaccurate posterior spread at intermediate sampling times. Our finite-sample posterior sampling approach is agnostic to the type of likelihood approximation and the type of (linear or nonlinear) forward model, and can thus serve as a drop-in diagnostic to evaluate the accuracy and failure modes of existing and future posterior samplers.

</details>


### [334] [Fairness-Aware Federated Learning with Trajectory Shapley Value](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30336)
*Daniel Kuznetsov,Ziqi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于轨迹Shapley值（TSV）的联邦学习聚合框架FedTSV，通过动态评估客户端对模型优化路径的影响并自适应调整权重，有效提升了联邦学习的公平性、稳定性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的联邦学习聚合方案通常采用固定权重，无法准确反映客户端数据异构性和时变贡献差异，导致模型训练存在偏见、不稳定以及对恶意参与者缺乏鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“轨迹Shapley值”（Trajectory Shapley Value, TSV）的贡献度度量方法，该方法通过验证集评估客户端对全局模型优化轨迹的影响；并基于TSV设计了FedTSV聚合算法，实现根据客户端实时表现动态调整聚合权重。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的实验结果表明，FedTSV能够加速模型收敛，提升系统鲁棒性，并提供更具公平性的贡献评估，显著优于传统的聚合策略。

Conclusion: 本文提出的FedTSV框架通过引入轨迹Shapley值，有效解决了联邦学习中客户端贡献度评估不公平及权重固定的问题，为实现公平、鲁棒且高效的联邦优化提供了新的理论与实践视角。

Abstract: Federated learning is an emerging distributed paradigm that addresses the challenges posed by heterogeneous, privacy-sensitive data. It enables multiple clients to train a model collaboratively by aggregating their local updates at a server. However, conventional aggregation schemes typically use fixed weights that fail to reflect unequal and time-varying client contributions, leading to biased and unstable learning. To improve fairness and stability, we propose the Trajectory Shapley Value (TSV), a contribution metric that evaluates how each client influences the optimization trajectory of the global model using a validation-based, temporally consistent utility. Building on TSV, we design FedTSV, an adaptive aggregation method that converts per-round evaluations into dynamic client weights, allowing the server to respond to heterogeneous and adversarial participation in real time. Experiments on benchmark datasets show that FedTSV accelerates convergence, improves robustness, and yields more equitable contribution assessments, thereby providing a principled foundation for fairness-aware federated optimization.

</details>


### [335] [Efficient Test-Time Finetuning of LLMs via Convex Reconstruction and Gradient Caching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30337)
*Alaa Khamis,Alaa Maalouf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HullFT 是一种新型的测试时微调优化框架，通过几何投影和梯度复用技术，在保持高性能的同时大幅提升了模型针对单次查询的微调处理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时微调（TTFT）方法在执行效率与模型质量之间存在冲突：检索过程往往包含冗余信息，而为了提升质量引入的复杂多样性感知选择机制又带来了难以承受的单次查询开销，因此亟需一种既能保证效果又能大幅提升推理速度的新方案。

Method: 提出了一种基于几何原理的 HullFT 方法：首先利用 Frank-Wolfe 优化算法将查询嵌入表示为训练序列的稀疏凸组合，以获取兼具相关性与多样性的支持集；随后通过几何整数化程序将分数权重转换为整数多重集，并结合“梯度复用”（Gradient Reuse）技术有效降低了重复样本微调时的计算开销。

Result: 实验结果表明，与当前最先进的 TTFT 方法相比，HullFT 在显著降低运行时间的同时，实现了更低的比特/字节（bits-per-byte）指标，从而在质量与效率的权衡（tradeoff）中取得了更优的表现。

Conclusion: HullFT 通过几何方法成功解决了测试时微调（TTFT）中的效率与质量平衡难题，证明了基于几何投影和梯度复用的优化策略在处理大规模数据检索与微调时具有显著的性能优势。

Abstract: Test-time finetuning (TTFT) is a rapidly evolving paradigm that adapts a language model to each prompt by retrieving related sequences, updating the model on them, and then evaluating the prompt. However, TTFT is only practical if it is fast: selection and finetuning both happen per query, making each a direct bottleneck. Existing methods trade speed for quality: fast retrieval is often redundant, while stronger diversity-aware selection adds prohibitive per-query cost. We introduce HullFT, a geometric approach to TTFT that addresses both bottlenecks. Given a query, HullFT first represents the query embedding as a sparse convex combination of few training sequences, using efficient projection-free Frank-Wolfe optimization. This yields a support set that is inherently relevant and diverse. We then convert the fractional convex weights into an exact integer multiset for finetuning through a geometric integerization procedure. The resulting multiplicities naturally create repeated examples, which we exploit with Gradient Reuse to amortize forward-backward computation across repeated finetuning steps. Our experiments show that HullFT improves the quality-efficiency tradeoff over current state-of-the-art TTFT methods, achieving lower bits-per-byte at substantially lower total runtime.

</details>

### [336] [On the Practice of Scaling Search Conversion Rate Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29232)
*James Pak,Jyun-Yu Jiang,Fan Zhang,Sen Wang,Taekmin Kim,Henry Tsai,Vijay Rajaram,Juexin Lin,Mohitdeep Singh,Alessandro Magnani,Johnny Chen,Qian Zhao,Rao Fu,Zhirong Liang,Jordan Gilliland,Winter Jiao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文研究了搜索转化率预测模型在扩容骨干计算、嵌入参数和数据量时的性能表现，提出了针对性的训练与推断优化方案，在保持低延迟的同时显著提升了模型预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高流量场景下，搜索转化率（CVR）预测模型需要在提升预测质量与严格限制训练成本及推断延迟之间取得平衡。现有研究缺乏针对模型规模化影响因素的系统性分析。

Method: 1. 经验性研究：分析骨干计算、嵌入参数规模和训练数据量对模型质量的影响；2. 架构评估：在真实大规模电商数据上测试多种模型架构及集成方案；3. 训练优化：采用简化的热启动（warmstart）策略加速训练；4. 推断优化：利用解耦图执行（decoupled graph execution）和动态批处理（dynamic batching）实现低延迟GPU推断。

Result: 相比基准模型，新模型在增加2.5倍训练数据和8倍推断算力的情况下，保持了极低的延迟影响，在线A/B测试中搜索转化率提升了2.6%。

Conclusion: 通过合理选择模型骨干架构、解耦训练与推断的优化策略，能够在控制成本和推断延迟的前提下，通过扩容数据、参数和算力显著提升搜索转化率预测模型的性能。

Abstract: Scaling a Search Conversion Rate (CVR) prediction model, especially in high-traffic environments, presents a challenge: superior model quality needs to be balanced with strict constraints on training cost and serving latency. This paper details an effective approach for scaling modern search CVR prediction models. We begin with an empirical study to understand the scaling performance of search CVR models, analyzing how quality improves as we scale three key factors of model backbone computation, the size of embedding parameters, and the volume of training data.
  We use a large-scale production dataset, comprising over a year of customer interaction logs from a high-traffic e-commerce platform, to evaluate the scalability of several state-of-the-art architectures and their ensembles. Our key findings are: (1) selecting the right backbone and scaling factors is crucial; (2) the impact of scaling backbone, embedding, and data is largely independent and additive, which has implications for more efficient scaling exploration; (3) a streamlined warmstart strategy can accelerate training iterations while simplifying new updates; (4) inference optimization strategies such as decoupled graph execution and dynamic batching can enable low-latency GPU serving even for high-capacity models. Compared to a baseline of a pre-scaling production model, we ultimately deployed a model trained on 2.5x larger training data with 8x more inference compute while having minimal latency impact. Online A/B tests also demonstrate that our launches achieved a combined +2.6% gain in a key metric of search conversion rate.

</details>


### [337] [CrossAlpha: An Annual-Report Benchmark for Cross-Market Factor Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29286)
*Qian Wang,Zhongyi Tong,Nuo Chen,Zhaomin Wu,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文推出了CrossAlpha，这是首个面向跨市场金融因子研究的公开年报基准，通过标准化多市场披露信息和严格的时间对齐机制，显著提升了利用全球跨市场信息预测股票收益的研究能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的金融研究基准无法支持跨市场披露信息对收益预测的研究。跨市场研究面临语言和监管差异、通用报告成分带来的偏差、以及交易时间对齐等技术挑战，缺乏一个统一的评估标准。

Method: 1. 披露蒸馏（Disclosure Distillation）：将多语言、异构的年报文件标准化为统一的十类英语商业描述；2. 残差模式图构建（Residual Schema Graph Construction）：利用PCA白化技术去除公共报告成分，计算跨市场公司对的相似度评分；3. 时间对齐评估（Timing-Aligned Evaluation）：结合11年的日频行情数据，在考虑实际跨市场执行限制的前提下构建收益预测任务。

Result: CrossAlpha涵盖了美、日、台、韩、港5个市场约3600家公司的1.07万份年报。实验表明，基于披露信息的跨市场关联在预测能力上优于传统的行业代码和收益相关性基准（例如在美国到日本的设置中，ICIR达到0.39，远高于基准的0.07-0.18）。

Conclusion: CrossAlpha填补了跨市场金融研究中缺乏标准基准的空白，证明了跨市场披露信息在预测目标市场收益方面的有效性，为金融自然语言处理（NLP）领域提供了一个可复用、以收益为导向的研究平台。

Abstract: Cross-market factor research studies whether firm-level signals from one or more markets can predict returns in a target market, but existing public benchmarks do not support cross-market disclosure-to-return evaluation. Building such a benchmark is challenging because filings differ across languages and regulatory systems, disclosure-derived similarity can be biased by common reporting components, and cross-market signals must be evaluated under feasible trading-time alignment. We introduce \textbf{CrossAlpha}, a public annual-report benchmark for cross-market factor research. CrossAlpha addresses these challenges through three corresponding components: \emph{Disclosure Distillation}, which standardises heterogeneous filings into ten-category English business descriptions; \emph{Residual Schema Graph Construction}, which builds PCA-whitened cross-market firm-pair scores from schema-level disclosures; and \emph{Timing-Aligned Evaluation}, which pairs the graph with 11 years of daily OHLCV data to construct forward-return labels under feasible cross-market execution protocols. CrossAlpha covers about 3,600 firms and 10,700 firm-year reports from the United States, Japan, Taiwan, South Korea, and Hong Kong, and releases about 19M directed firm-pair scores. In experiments, disclosure-derived cross-market peers outperform domestic text, industry-code, and return-correlation peers in the US-to-Japan setting (ICIR 0.39 versus 0.07--0.18), and cross-market sources beat the domestic text baseline in most target markets. CrossAlpha offers an open-sourced, reusable, return-grounded benchmark for cross-market financial NLP.

</details>


### [338] [UniNote: A Unified Embedding Model for Multimodal Representation and Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29287)
*Jinghan Zhao,Wenwei Jin,Anqi Li,Jintao Tong,Luya Mo,Jiawei Li,Bin Li,Yao Hu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有工业级 Item-to-Item（I2I）检索中存在的挑战：难以平衡全局内容表示与细粒度局部检索、解耦式检索-排序流水线导致的效率低下，以及模型精度与服务延迟之间的固有权衡。

Method: 提出了 UniNote 模型，采用两阶段训练策略：第一阶段通过对比监督微调（Contrastive SFT）构建鲁棒的基础嵌入；第二阶段通过强化学习（RL）优化模型与内容相关性的对齐。此外，该模型集成了 Matryoshka 表示学习（MRL）以实现灵活的维度伸缩，提升了检索效率。

Result: UniNote 在多项 I2I 检索任务中达到了 SOTA 性能，并成功部署于小红书平台。实践表明，其在大幅提升检索质量的同时，显著降低了大规模应用中的算力成本。

Conclusion: UniNote 通过结合多模态统一嵌入与两阶段训练范式，有效解决了工业级 I2I 检索中细粒度表示、系统效率与部署延迟之间的矛盾，为大规模内容平台的检索架构提供了高效且高性能的解决方案。

Abstract: Item-to-Item (I2I) retrieval is a fundamental part of modern content platforms, supporting critical industrial workflows from recommendation engines to content auditing. While multimodal embedding methods have advanced general retrieval, they often falter in I2I scenarios due to the challenges of balancing global content representation with fine-grained local retrieval, the systemic inefficiency of decoupled embedding-and-ranking pipelines, and the inherent trade-offs between model precision and serving latency. To solve these issues, we propose \textbf{UniNote}, a unified embedding model designed for industrial I2I retrieval. Tailored retrieval strategies are introduced to support representation learning over complex, multimodal content at varying granularities. To operationalize these strategies, UniNote employs a two-stage training paradigm: the first stage leverages contrastive SFT to establish robust base embeddings, while the second stage refines ranking quality through a reinforcement learning (RL) process that aligns the model with content relevance. Our results show that UniNote achieves SOTA performance across diverse I2I tasks. Deployed at Xiaohongshu and integrated with Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL), UniNote achieved significant improvements in retrieval quality and cost efficiency in large-scale applications.

</details>


### [339] [ACE: Anisotropy-Controllable Embedding for LLM-enhanced Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29322)
*Dongcheol Lee,Hye-young Kim,Jongwuk Lee*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 为了解决大模型生成的推荐嵌入存在各向异性导致模型难以学习的问题，本文提出了ACE方法，通过线性自编码器平衡了嵌入的几何均匀性与语义保留，显著提升了顺序推荐的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的推荐系统（LLM-as-Extractor）生成的嵌入往往存在严重的各向异性（各向量方向高度重合），导致几何分布不平衡，难以有效地与协同过滤信号进行微调。

Method: 提出了一种名为ACE（Anisotropy-Controllable Embedding）的框架，利用线性自编码器（LAE）重塑嵌入分布；通过L2正则化控制维度分散性以降低各向异性，同时利用重构损失保持原始语义关系。

Result: 在多个数据集上的实验表明，ACE在Recall@20和NDCG@20指标上分别取得了最高12.4%和11.8%的性能提升，优于现有的LLM增强型顺序推荐模型。

Conclusion: ACE通过显式控制LLM生成嵌入的各向异性，有效提升了推荐系统的性能，证明了在将LLM应用于推荐任务时，对齐几何分布与语义结构的重要性。

Abstract: Recent advances in the LLM-as-Extractor paradigm leverage large language models (LLMs) to transfer semantically rich item embeddings into sequential recommendation (SR) backbones. However, LLM-generated embeddings often suffer from strong anisotropy. Most vectors are concentrated in similar directions, resulting in a geometric imbalance that makes it difficult to adapt to collaborative signals during fine-tuning. To address this challenge, we propose Anisotropy-Controllable Embedding (ACE), which explicitly controls the anisotropy of LLM-generated embeddings. Specifically, ACE utilizes a linear autoencoder (LAE) to reshape the embedding distribution while preserving its semantic structure. In this process, the L2-regularization term mitigates the anisotropy by controlling the dispersion of embedding dimensions, while the reconstruction loss maintains semantic relationships among items. That is, ACE balances geometric uniformity and semantic embedding preservation for more stable learning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ACE consistently outperforms existing LLM-enhanced SR models, yielding improvements of up to 12.4% and 11.8% in Recall@20 and NDCG@20, respectively.

</details>


### [340] [Latent Terms: Dense Retrievers Contain Trivially Extractable BM25-ready Zipfian Vocabularies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29384)
*Benjamin Clavié,Sean Lee,Aamir Shakir,Makoto P. Kato*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需额外训练目标的“潜在词项”方法，通过稀疏自编码器从任意稠密检索器中提取稀疏特征，在实现高效稀疏检索的同时，显著提升了模型在复杂检索任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稠密检索模型虽表现出色，但其评分函数可能未能充分挖掘模型内部表示的表达能力。作者旨在验证稠密检索器学到的表示是否可以分解为可用的稀疏特征，从而实现无需特定稀疏训练目标的稀疏检索。

Method: 提出了一种名为“潜在词项（Latent Terms）”的方法，利用稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoders）对冻结的稠密检索器的表示进行分解，提取出具有Zipf分布特征的稀疏特征词汇表，并直接应用于BM25风格的经典稀疏检索评分。

Result: 该方法不仅能与基础稠密模型及类似的SPLADE变体效果持平甚至更优，还在专门针对单向量检索缺陷的LIMIT任务上显著优于基础稠密模型，证明了其在无需稀疏检索监督的情况下仍具备极高的检索性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，稠密检索器内部蕴含着比其默认评分函数所展示的更为丰富和可索引的结构。通过稀疏自编码器提取“潜在词项（Latent Terms）”，不仅能使稠密模型在无需额外监督的情况下实现稀疏检索，还能提升模型处理复杂检索任务的能力。

Abstract: We propose Latent Terms, a method revealing that models trained for dense retrieval, whether single- or multi-vector, learn representations that can trivially be decomposed into retrieval-ready sparse features. When trained on frozen retrievers, Sparse Autoencoders without any retrieval-specific adjustments extract a latent vocabulary with approximately Zipfian collection statistics, directly suitable for classical sparse retrieval scoring via BM25. This approach enables sparse retrieval while requiring no learned expansion objective or sparse retrieval supervision whatsoever, and can be readily applied to any dense retriever. Latent Terms is able to match or outperform single-vector scoring methods from its own base model as well as comparable SPLADE variants. In addition, it substantially outperforms its base model on LIMIT, a task specifically designed to highlight the failures of single-vector retrieval. Overall, our results highlight that neural retrievers contain more expressive and indexable structure than their default scoring functions expose, but that other methods can nonetheless be leveraged.

</details>


### [341] [FLASH-MAXSIM: IO-Aware Fused Kernels for Late-Interaction Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29517)
*Roi Pony,Adi Raz Goldfarb,Idan Friedman,Daniel Ezer,Udi Barzelay*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Flash-MaxSim 是一种高效的 GPU 计算内核，通过避免存储大型中间相似度张量，大幅提升了 ColBERT 等后期交互检索模型的计算速度并降低了显存消耗，同时确保了排序结果的精确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 ColBERT/ColPali 类后期交互（Late-interaction）检索模型在计算 MaxSim 时，会产生巨大的中间相似度张量，这极大地消耗了 GPU 显存并限制了批处理规模，在处理大规模文档集时成为了计算瓶颈。

Method: 提出了一种 IO 感知型融合 GPU 核函数（Flash-MaxSim），通过将查询和文档的分块流式传输到片上 SRAM 中进行计算，在计算过程中直接进行行最大值归约，从而避免了中间相似度张量的显存实例化。此外，该方法还包括反向传播的 IO 感知优化、INT8xINT8 量化以及支持变长（无填充）评分机制。

Result: 在 A100 GPU 上比普通 PyTorch 实现快 3.9 倍（H100 上快 4.7 倍），推理显存占用降低高达 16 倍，训练显存占用降低约 28 倍，并保持了与 FP32 参考实现 100% 的前 20 位排序一致性。

Conclusion: Flash-MaxSim 通过 IO 感知型融合核函数技术，成功消除了计算 MaxSim 时对 GPU 显存的大量需求，在保持完全相同数学精度的前提下，实现了显著的性能提升和显存占用降低，为大规模模型的高效推理与训练提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Late-interaction retrieval (ColBERT, ColPali) scores a query against a document with the MaxSim operator: for every query token, the maximum similarity over the document tokens, summed over
  query tokens. The standard implementation materializes the full query-token x document-token similarity tensor in GPU memory; for visual ColPali at 10K documents this tensor alone is 21 GB in
  FP16, created only to be reduced to one score per document and discarded. It exhausts a 40 GB GPU and bounds the achievable batch size in both inference and training. We present
  Flash-MaxSim, an IO-aware fused GPU kernel that computes exactly the same scores without ever materializing the tensor, by streaming query and document tiles through on-chip SRAM and folding
  the row-maximum reduction into the same pass. We extend the IO-aware principle through the training backward pass, an inverse-grid CSR construction that reuses the forward argmax for an
  atomic-free, destination-owned gradient reduction, and through INT8xINT8 quantization and variable-length (padding-free) scoring. Flash-MaxSim is up to 3.9x faster on an A100 (4.7x on an
  H100) than naive PyTorch at matched precision, uses up to 16x less inference memory and ~28x less training memory, unlocks corpus and batch sizes that exhaust PyTorch entirely, preserves the
  exact ranking (100% top-20 agreement with an FP32 reference)

</details>


### [342] [Rec-Distill: An Industrial Distillation Pipeline for Large-Scale Recommendation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29755)
*Haoran Ding,Wenlin Zhao,Yuchen Jiang,Juren Li,Jie Zhu,Xinchun Li,Yishujie Zhao,Yi Zhang,Ao Qiao,Jianhui Dong,Cheng Chen,Ziyan Gong,Deping Xie,Peng Xu,Zikai Wang,Yuwei Wang,Huizhi Yang,Zhe Chen,Yuchao Zheng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大规模推荐模型难以部署的痛点，Rec-Distill 框架通过一系列高效的蒸馏策略，将超大规模教师模型的知识迁移至轻量级学生模型，实现了性能与效率的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模推荐模型在遵循缩放定律（Scaling Laws）时性能优异，但受限于工业生产环境对模型推理效率和延迟的严格要求，难以直接部署，导致离线性能增长与在线部署需求之间存在本质矛盾。

Method: 提出了一套工业级知识蒸馏流水线，包含以下核心技术：1. 解耦训练（Decoupled Training）；2. 黑盒蒸馏（Black-box Distillation）；3. 去偏机制（Debiasing Mechanism）；4. 用于动态环境的混合批处理-流式处理流水线（Hybrid batch-streaming pipeline）。

Result: 在多个工业推荐与广告场景中，将教师模型参数扩展至24B，行为序列长度达20K；蒸馏后的轻量化学生模型成功捕获了教师模型的大部分性能增益，最高蒸馏迁移率超过60%，并在实际业务指标上取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: Rec-Distill 为工业级推荐系统提供了一套实用的框架，成功弥合了离线大规模模型缩放与在线轻量化部署之间的鸿沟，证明了知识蒸馏是实现超大规模推荐模型落地应用的有效路径。

Abstract: Large recommendation models have demonstrated substantial potential gains under scaling laws, yet these gains are difficult to realize in industrial recommendation systems because real-world deployment requires lightweight models with strict serving efficiency and latency guarantees. This creates a fundamental gap between offline model scaling and online deployment. In this work, we present Rec-Distill, an industrial distillation pipeline that transfers the performance gains of large-scale recommendation modeling to efficient serving models. Rec-Distill combines large-teacher scaling with student-side transfer optimization through decoupled training, black-box distillation, debiasing mechanism, and a hybrid batch-streaming pipeline for dynamic recommendation environments. Across multiple recommendation and advertising scenarios on real-world platforms, our framework scales teacher models up to 24B dense parameters and 20K behavior sequence length, while enabling lightweight students to recover a substantial portion of teacher gains, with distillation transferability exceeding 60% in the best setting. Extensive offline and online experiments further show that these transferred gains consistently translate into measurable business improvements under industrial constraints. These results demonstrate that Rec-Distill provides a practical framework for distilling large-scale recommendation models into deployable, cost-efficient serving systems, while also establishing a reliable path toward scaling recommendation models to even larger regimes in the future.

</details>


### [343] [Uncertainty Quantification for Multimodal Retrieval Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29956)
*Simon Binz,Heydar Soudani,Faegheh Hasibi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对多模态 RAG 系统中不确定性量化不足的问题，提出了一种名为 LeMUQ 的可学习框架，通过分析输入修改下的概率信号来提升模型输出可靠性的评估能力，在多项指标上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管检索增强生成（RAG）与视觉语言模型（VLM）结合提升了多模态问答能力，但生成的答案仍存在不准确或误导性的问题。现有的不确定性量化方法多针对纯文本模型，在处理涉及检索、视觉理解和生成的复杂多模态 RAG 流程时表现不佳，因此需要专门针对多模态环境的不确定性量化方案。

Method: 作者提出了 LeMUQ（可学习多模态不确定性量化）方法。该方法通过在输入修改（如移除模态或检索到的上下文）下分析 token 的概率分布，提取多模态和检索感知的概率信号；随后将这些信号编码为“概率 token”，并利用一个微调后的模型来处理这些信息，从而捕捉模态与检索过程之间的复杂相互作用，进而评估输出的可靠性。

Result: 实验结果表明，LeMUQ 在多个数据集、检索器和 VLM 模型上均优于现有的基准及微调方法，平均将 AUROC 指标提升了 3.8%。此外，该方法在不同检索配置和数据集上展现了良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 LeMUQ 框架有效地量化了多模态 RAG 系统中的不确定性，证明了结合多模态特征与检索上下文对于提升模型可靠性的重要性，为构建更安全、更可信的多模态问答系统提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) improves the question answering capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) by incorporating external knowledge and has recently been extended to multimodal settings through Vision-Language Models (VLMs) that integrate visual and textual information. Despite these advances, generated answers can still be incorrect or misleading. Uncertainty Quantification (UQ) methods aim to estimate the reliability of model outputs, but most existing approaches are designed for text-only models and perform poorly in multimodal RAG scenarios. A key challenge is capturing uncertainty arising from multiple stages of the pipeline, including retrieval, visual understanding, and generation. In this work, we show that modeling uncertainty using multimodal and retrieval-aware probability signals improves estimation in multimodal RAG systems. We introduce LeMUQ, a Learnable Multimodal UQ method that analyzes token probabilities under input modifications, such as removing modalities or retrieved context. By encoding these signals as probability tokens and processing them with a finetuned model, our approach captures interactions between modalities and retrieval. Experiments across datasets, retrievers, and VLMs show consistent improvements over baseline and finetuned UQ methods. Our proposed LeMUQ increases the AUROC metric by 3.8% on average. Additionally, our method shows strong generalization performance across different retrieval setups and datasets with mixed results when transferring across different VLMs. Our findings highlight the importance of modeling multimodal uncertainty and provide a step toward more reliable and safer multimodal RAG systems. Code is available on GitHub.

### [344] [No More K-means:Single-Stage Sparse Coding for Efficient Multi-Vector Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30120)
*Lixuan Guo,Yifei Wang,Tiansheng Wen,Aosong Feng,Stefanie Jegelka,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种名为SSR的稀疏检索新范式，通过稀疏自动编码器将标记嵌入转化为高维稀疏表示，实现了在无需复杂聚类的情况下提升检索速度和精度，显著优于传统多向量检索模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多向量检索模型（如ColBERT）虽精度高，但因保存大量标记向量而面临巨大的存储和计算瓶颈。为缓解这一问题，现有方案通常采用降维和聚类，但这导致了高昂的索引延迟以及语义信息的压缩损失。因此，需要一种既能保持细粒度交互优势，又能降低计算开销的新方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为单阶段稀疏检索（SSR）的新范式，使用稀疏自动编码器（SAE）将细粒度的标记嵌入（token embeddings）映射为高维且高度稀疏的表示，从而彻底摒弃了传统的K-means聚类，并结合倒排索引技术实现高效检索。

Result: 在BEIR基准测试中，SSR表现优异：索引时间相比ColBERTv2缩短了15倍，检索延迟降低了一半，同时检索准确率也优于现有的先进基准模型。

Conclusion: SSR通过稀疏编码成功打破了多向量检索中存储与效率的权衡限制，证明了利用高维稀疏表示替代传统的聚类方法是实现高性能信息检索的可行且高效的途径，为大规模语义搜索提供了新的技术范式。

Abstract: Multi-vector retrieval (MVR) models, exemplified by ColBERT, have established new benchmarks in retrieval accuracy by preserving fine-grained token-level interactions. However, this granularity imposes prohibitive storage and retrieval efficiency bottlenecks: to manage the immense memory footprint and computational overhead of billion-scale token vectors, state-of-the-art systems are forced to rely on aggressive dimension reduction and complex clustering (e.g., K-means). This compromise introduces two critical limitations: excessive indexing latency of clustering large-scale corpora and semantic information loss inherent to compression. In this paper, we propose Single-stage Sparse Retrieval (SSR}, a paradigm shift that replaces expensive clustering with efficient sparse coding. Instead of compressing features into low-dimensional dense vectors, we utilize Sparse Autoencoder (SAE) to project token embeddings into a high-dimensional but highly sparse representation. This transformation enables us to bypass vector clustering entirely and leverage inverted indexing for precise, high-throughput retrieval. Extensive experiments on the BEIR benchmark demonstrate that SSR achieves a "trifecta" of improvements: it reduces indexing time by 15x compared to ColBERTv2, halves retrieval latency, and simultaneously improves retrieval performance over leading baselines.

### [345] [LexPath: A domain-oriented multi-path framework for legal article retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30205)
*Weixuan Liu,Qingfeng Zhuge,Xuyang Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的开放域检索方法过度依赖表面词汇或语义相似度，难以区分在文本上相似但在法律适用上不相关或意图不符的法条，导致法律 AI 系统难以实现真正的“有据可依”。

Method: 提出了一种名为 LexPath 的领域导向多路径框架：1. 多路径检索模块：结合了 IRAC（问题-规则-分析-结论）引导的稀疏路径（关键词扩展）和结构引导的稠密路径（利用法律层级和引用关系挖掘难负样本）。2. 意图感知重排模块：通过评估查询与法条之间的意图一致性分数，对初步检索结果进行精细化排序。

Result: 在两个公开基准数据集和一个自建的专业领域数据集上，LexPath 的检索性能均优于现有的词汇检索、稠密检索、混合检索以及自适应 RAG 基线模型。消融实验证实了框架中各组件的有效性。

Conclusion: LexPath 通过多路径检索和意图感知重排，显著提升了法律法条检索的准确性和专业性。该研究证明了整合法律结构信息与用户意图对于构建可追溯、可靠的法律 AI 系统至关重要。

Abstract: Legal article retrieval is critical for building traceable and reliable legal AI systems, where conclusions must be grounded in specific legal articles. However, existing open-domain retrieval methods rely heavily on surface-level lexical or semantic similarity, making it difficult for them to distinguish legally relevant articles from those that are textually similar but legally inapplicable or misaligned with the user's underlying intent. To bridge this gap, we propose \textsc{LexPath}, a domain-oriented multi-path framework comprising a multi-path retrieval module and an intent-aware reranking module. The retrieval module combines two complementary legal-specific paths to collect candidate articles: an IRAC-guided sparse path that expands queries with legally informative keywords, and a structure-guided dense path trained with hard negatives derived from legal hierarchy and citation relations. Then, the reranking module further refines the candidate ranking by incorporating the intent consistency score between queries and legal articles. We evaluate \textsc{LexPath} on two publicly available benchmarks focusing on general-public queries and a self-constructed benchmark targeting domain-professional scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate that \textsc{LexPath} consistently outperforms lexical, dense, hybrid, and adaptive retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) baselines. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of each component.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: GRASP 是一个三阶段检索框架：1. 基于规划的图检索（利用图结构生成查询路径）；2. 计划条件化融合（将图检索结果与密集检索器结合）；3. 针对融合候选集的微调重排序器。

Result: GRASP 在 STaRK 基准测试的所有指标上均实现了显著提升，平均 Hit@1 从 62.0 提高到 73.9，展现了优于现有最先进（SOTA）方法的性能。

Existing hybrid retrieval systems on SKBs either use the graph only for query expansion, mix textual and structural branches under a global weighting, or rely on fine-tuned graph-traversal generators. We present GRASP, a three-stage SKB retrieval framework unifying plan-based graph retrieval, plan-conditioned fusion with a dense retriever, and a fine-tuned reranker over the fused candidates. GRASP substantially advances the state of the art on every metric across the three STaRK benchmarks, lifting average Hit@1 from 62.0 to 73.9. Ablation and sensitivity studies further confirm the effectiveness and robustness of GRASP.

### [347] [Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation via Implicit Reasoning in Amap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28888)
*Sicong Wang,Ruiting Dong,Yue Liu,Bowen Zheng,Jun Meng,Jie Li,Shuaijun Guo,Yu Gu,Fanyi Di,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 为解决LLM在时空意图序列推荐中部署难、延迟高的问题，本文提出了GPlan框架，通过隐式思维链蒸馏和时空反事实DPO训练轻量级模型，实现了高效且符合现实约束的意图序列生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界的用户行为呈现时空依赖的意图流。大语言模型（LLM）虽具备强推理能力，但直接部署于工业推荐场景时面临推理延迟高、计划缺乏物理可行性及上下文不匹配等挑战。为此，研究旨在设计一种既能保持LLM推理深度，又能满足工业级实时响应要求的轻量化生成框架。

Method: 1. 渐进式隐式思维链蒸馏（Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation）：将大模型的显式推理过程压缩为预留的隐层标记（latent tokens），使小模型在无需生成长文本的情况下继承复杂的规划逻辑。2. 时空反事实直接偏好优化（Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO）：利用反事实上下文-计划对进行对齐训练，强化模型对时空约束的感知，减少不切实际的规划生成。

Result: 离线实验与在线A/B测试结果表明，GPlan能够有效提升推荐序列的逻辑连贯性和对时空环境的响应能力，在满足严格时延约束的同时优于对比模型。

Conclusion: GPlan框架通过蒸馏和对齐技术，成功将LLM的复杂推理能力迁移至轻量级模型，在保证推理时延和物理约束满足的前提下，显著提升了生成式时空意图序列推荐的逻辑连贯性和上下文响应能力。

Abstract: Real-world user behavior rarely consists of isolated actions; instead, it often forms intent flows governed by spatiotemporal dependencies. To provide integrated service recommendations, we focus on the task of Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation (GSISR), which aims to generate intent sequences that are logically coherent and physically executable within complex spatiotemporal contexts. While LLMs offer strong reasoning potential for GSISR, direct industrial deployment is limited by high inference latency and context-mismatched or physically infeasible plans. To address these challenges, we propose a generative framework, GPlan, that internalizes LLM reasoning into lightweight models through two components. First, to enable reasoning under strict latency constraints, we introduce Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation, which compresses explicit reasoning processes into reserved latent tokens, allowing small models to inherit complex planning logic without generating long reasoning text. Second, to address the disconnect between general knowledge and real-world constraints, we design Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO. By aligning the model with counterfactual context-plan pairs, we improve sensitivity to spatiotemporal context and reduce context-mismatched plans. Offline experiments and online A/B testing demonstrate that our approach improves sequence coherence and context responsiveness. Our implementation and the anonymized GSISR dataset are available at https://github.com/alibaba/GPlan.

### [348] [Toward User Preference Alignment in LLM Recommendation via Explicit Context Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29141)
*Weizhi Zhang,Wooseong Yang,Yuxin Cui,Zhaohui Guo,Hins Hu,Liangwei Yang,Henry Peng Zou,Qifei Wang,Hanqing Zeng,Jiayi Liu,Yinglong Xia,Philip S. Yu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文通过综述推荐系统的演进历程，分析了显式反馈的价值，并提出了整合用户显式信号到可扩展的大语言模型（LLM）推荐系统中的框架，同时呼吁建立新的基准测试和评估指标。

Result: 文章指出显式反馈能够有效缓解偏好对齐偏差和过滤气泡问题，为实现更精准、多样化且可解释的推荐系统提供了新的路径。

Conclusion: 本文强调了从隐式行为数据向利用显式文本上下文数据的范式转移，主张将显式反馈整合到下一代大模型驱动的推荐系统中，以实现更具透明度、解释性和个性化的推荐服务。

In addition, it offers critical heterogeneous information for user preference alignment and more explainable recommendations. Overlooking such signals can lead to misaligned user preferences and further reinforce filter bubbles, as algorithms fail to understand the "semantic context" behind user choices. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) present new opportunities to harness user-generated content for more accurate and diverse recommendations, yet current LLM-based recommendations still focus on using item meta-data and underutilize this resource. In this paper, we advocate for prioritizing explicit context feedback in the next generation of LLM-based RecSys. We review the evolution of recommendation paradigms, highlight the value of context-rich feedback, call for new benchmarks and metrics, and introduce frameworks for integrating explicit user signals into scalable LLM-driven RecSys. Centering on user-preference modeling, we aim to foster more personalized, transparent, and explainable RecSys online platforms.
